California News - The Pan-American Inter-Commercial Conference opened on the 25th of this month in Sacramento, California, with a total of twenty-two participating countries, including the United States. This conference was initiated by the Sacramento Local Civic Association, and the opening session was chaired by Mr. Lubin, the chairman of the Civic Association. Representatives from South American countries included governors, importers and exporters, leaders in the business community, as well as U.S. senators and key figures in the business world. This conference had been in preparation for nine months since its inception. Invitation letters were sent to South American countries on December 16, 1929, requesting them to send representatives to the conference. The conference venue was located in the California State Capitol Building. During the opening session, California Governor Young delivered a speech, welcoming representatives from various countries. National flags of various countries were hung throughout the conference venue. According to Governor Young, "The main purpose of convening the Pan-American Inter-Commercial Conference is to discuss the possibility of encouraging commerce among the countries of the Americas. However, if the conference can foster closer relationships and better understanding among the business representatives present, then this conference will be of great value." The conference will continue until the 30th. On September 1st, the American Western States Agricultural and Industrial Exhibition will follow, showcasing agricultural and industrial products from the Western States for the representatives from South American countries to observe. Mr. Lubin, the chairman of the Civic Association, stated, "Regarding this conference, not only does the Pacific coast deeply feel that it contains unlimited opportunities, but the entire United States, even the Atlantic coast, is paying close attention and will send representatives here to discuss mutual exchange of commerce with South American individuals." (World)

Soviet Union

Communist International Trade Union Congress

Resolves to Expand Revolutionary Propaganda

Reuters, Riga, 26th - The Fifth World Congress of the Communist International Trade Union is currently being held in Moscow. A resolution has been passed, stating that the organizations represented by the Union have not received sufficient assistance in overseas strikes. Therefore, it demands that the Central Committee of the International Trade Union actively raise a special international strike fund to assist foreign labor unrest. The Congress also passed a resolution, recording the International Trade Union's attention to Black people's organizations. This resolution contains instructions to conduct revolutionary propaganda in Africa, America, South America, and the West Indies in a systematic way.

The Japanese Privy Council's Third Detailed Examination Meeting

Presents Six Questions to the Government

Approval of the Naval Treaty Still Needs Time

(Telegraphic dispatch from Tokyo, 27th) The third detailed examination committee held a meeting at 1:00 PM yesterday. Committee Chairman Ito designated Kaneko Kentaro to begin questioning: (1) What is the basis for Japan's defense expenditure, which is determined to be 70% of that of the United States? (2) Is it true that the Japanese plenipotentiary delegation declared three major principles in Washington on their way to England? (3) Please explain the important inquiries and responses exchanged between the Japanese government and the plenipotentiaries during the London Conference. (4) Was the conclusion of the meetings and negotiations between plenipotentiaries Matsudaira and Ri Da the American proposal or a compromise proposal? (5) During the inquiries, what kind of compromises did Plenipotentiary Zaibu attempt to make with the Naval General Staff? Is this true? (6) When abandoning the three major principles and making concessions, what kind of measures were taken? The questions involved minute details. Foreign Minister Shidehara gave a detailed account of the diplomatic process. Naval Minister Zaibu described the subtle negotiations that led to the unavoidable abandonment of the three major principles. Prime Minister Hamaguchi strongly defended Naval Minister Zaibu's actions from the perspectives of diplomatic relations and finance. After the answers were completed, Committee members Kawai and Kuroda wanted to continue questioning, but Committee Chairman Ito proposed that it was too hot today and that the questioning should be suspended for now. It was decided that the fourth committee meeting would be held at 1:00 PM on the 28th, and the meeting adjourned. Today's meeting was Kaneko Kentaro's solo performance and can be seen as a reconnaissance battle for the issue of supreme command. (Telegraphic dispatch from Tokyo, 27th) Only the three ministers attended the fourth detailed examination committee, entering into a genuine questioning battle. Given this situation, it will be difficult to hold a formal meeting of the Privy Council at the beginning of September. Even if it proceeds smoothly, it will be at the end of September or the beginning of October. The government said that even if the British mainland approves it, Ireland must convene parliament in November to give its support. The completion of British approval will be considerably delayed, so a slight delay in the Privy Council's deliberation is not a problem.

Trial Opens for Plot to Bomb German Parliament

Defendant Steadfastly Refuses to Speak

(Dispatch from Berlin from the National News Agency, 26th) After fifteen months of investigation, the trial for the plot to bomb the German Parliament last spring has opened in the Hamburg court. However, all twenty-one defendants steadfastly refuse to speak. They also refuse to answer questions from their lawyers. Therefore, after the prosecutor finished his statement, he withdrew from the court. The interrogating officer will consider whether the defendants' confessions during the police investigation can be used as evidence. The defendants are all radical nationalistic farmers' movement members who claim that the court cannot treat them fairly and will continue to refuse to speak.

Important News

Capital Citizens' Victory Celebration

The citizens of the capital, because the Central Army has recovered Jinan, and military victories are frequent, and the Communists in Hunan, Hubei and Jiangxi are being eliminated by the Central Army, which is a blessing for the future of the Party and the nation, will hold a victory celebration at the Public Stadium at 9:00 AM on the 27th.

Capital Victory Celebration Photograph 1

The meeting was attended by more than 10,000 people from various levels of party headquarters, agencies, and agricultural, industrial, commercial, academic, women's and other groups, presided over by Shi Weihuan, executive member of the Nanjing Municipal Party Headquarters, who delivered the opening remarks, stating that the Central Army had abandoned Jinan due to strategic considerations a month ago, luring the enemy deep, and at that time rumors arose, and the general public could not help but doubt the strength of the Central Army. At the same time, the Communist Party of Hunan, Hubei and Jiangxi, also colluding with the Northern warlords and the Reorganization Clique, took the opportunity to cause disturbances. Fortunately, our officers and soldiers bravely advanced, with one acting as a hundred, and finally achieved strategic success. Jinan has been recovered, and the main force of the Jin rebel army has collapsed and become disorganized. Recently, our army took advantage of the victory to advance and has reached Yucheng, taking the offensive to Pingyuan and Dezhou. The elimination of the rebel movement is not far off, and the obstacle has been removed, and unification is not difficult to achieve. This is truly something to be celebrated by the country and the people. Now the people of the country have understood the principle of those who obey survive and those who rebel perish, and they have also recognized the abundance of the central government's power. The international perspective has also greatly changed. In the past, imperialists held a wait-and-see attitude towards diplomacy, with no sincerity to resolve issues, and frequently made propaganda unfavorable to the central government, hoping to form a united front with warlords and all reactionary forces of the Communist Party. Now that the rebel forces have been defeated one by one, they are gradually expressing their approach to the diplomatic authorities, wanting to resolve all diplomatic issues. All of this is the good result of the efforts and sacrifices of the officers and soldiers at the front. All of our comrades and compatriots should admire them and express twelve points of grief for the generals and soldiers who are selfless and gave their lives in battle. In the future, we should work together towards the path of peaceful unification, eliminate internal strife forever, and do our best to deal with foreign affairs, to save the country, and to rescue the people, etc. At this time, the citizens of the entire venue observed three minutes of silence for the deceased generals and soldiers. Next, Yang Xiji, representative of the National Government, gave a speech, recounting the crimes of the Yan, Feng, and Wang rebel parties, hoping to eliminate all counter-revolutionary forces in the shortest possible time and ensure that there will be no successors to Yan, Feng, and Wang in the future, so as to use force to guarantee domestic unification, so that we can obtain a free and equal position in the international community. Next, Li Yuanbai of the Nanjing Municipal Party Headquarters gave a speech, saying that in this recovery of Jinan, the officers and soldiers at the front had each embraced the determination to sacrifice, and their loyalty and bravery were commendable. The achievements of Comrade Yang Jie, who designed the crossing of the Dawen River, and Comrade Xia Douyin, who firmly defended the city of Qufu, are especially unforgettable.

Capital Victory Celebration Photograph 1

The military operations on the Jinpu and Longhai Pinghan Railways have all achieved related victories, and the success of suppressing the rebellion is just around the corner. However, the harm of the Communist Party to the nation must be eradicated with all our efforts in the future. The Communist Party uses farmers and workers to cause disturbances, and countless farmers and workers have been sacrificed by them. It is hoped that everyone will pay attention to legitimate movements in the future and not be deceived by them. Next, Liu Luyin, representative of the Central Party Headquarters, gave a speech, with the main points being: (1) Eradicating Wang Jingwei and the remnants of the warlords, Communist Party, and Reorganization Clique who colluded with Wang. (2) Resisting the imperialists' secret assistance to the rebels and exposing their conspiracy. (3) Not being confused by counter-propaganda newspapers and eliminating reactionary remarks. Next, Wu Qingrong, representative of the Nanjing Municipal Government, Yi Ao, representative of the Two Lakes, Cheng Bingkun, representative of the labor union, and Mu Huaxuan, representative of the business community, all gave speeches. Then, the chairman announced the proposals: (1) A telegram of condolences to Commander-in-Chief Chiang and the anti-rebel generals and soldiers at the front. (2) A request to the central government and a letter to the National Government to thoroughly eliminate the remaining forces of the Yan and Feng warlords. (3) A telegram to Commander-in-Chief Chiang requesting that a large army be sent to annihilate the communist bandits as soon as possible. (4) A circular telegram to the whole country, upholding justice and denouncing the rebels Yan, Feng, Wang, Zou, and the communist bandits. (5) A request to the central government and a letter to the National Government to earnestly clarify officialdom, implement political tutelage, alleviate the people's plight, and lay the foundation for the country. The meeting unanimously passed the proposals and then dispersed after shouting slogans.

Song Ziwen Talks

The Process of Establishing the Salt Revenue Loan

(Dispatch from Hankou) Since Finance Minister Song Ziwen came to Hankou, his only task has been to complete the salt revenue loan and solicit short-term customs treasury bonds. The outside world does not know much about the situation of his contacts with various parties in recent days. Yesterday, a reporter from a certain agency visited him for an interview, and Mr. Song gave a very detailed conversation. The records of his answers are as follows: Reporter (Q): It was recently heard that the third salt revenue loan from Hubei banks is 3 million yuan. Thanks to your negotiations with the commercial banking group, the contract will be signed today (25th). Can you tell us the main points of the contract? Song (A): The salt revenue loan will indeed be signed today, with a loan amount of 3 million yuan, fully underwritten by the local commercial banking groups. It will be secured by 5 million yuan in promissory notes issued by the Hubei Salt Transport Bureau (i.e., issuing 1 million yuan in promissory notes each month from December this year to April next year). The interest rate is 1.2% per month. The aforementioned loan will be delivered to the national treasury in full in seven installments (every five days) starting from September 1st. Starting from September 1st, the commercial banks will jointly elect representatives to be stationed at the bureau to collect taxes and repay each bank on a bi-weekly basis. Regardless of the Hubei salt revenue, the principal and interest of the aforementioned loan should be fully repaid before April next year. (Q): The use of the aforementioned loan will naturally be to cover military expenses. However, the previous second Huai Salt loan of 3 million yuan and the refined salt loan of 1 million yuan were also mortgaged with salt revenue. How will the remaining balances be repaid? (A): Of the old debts, only 100,000 to 200,000 yuan are still owed from the 3 million yuan, and it will be repaid in full with principal and interest by the end of this month. The remaining balance of the 1 million yuan refined salt loan will be repaid by the national treasury by the end of November to clear the procedures. (Q): It is heard that the Hubei Finance Commissioner's Office collects national taxes, originally scheduled to collect more than 2.6 million yuan per month, and the office pays 2.51 million yuan per month for the Central Army's expenses here. In recent months, the income has decreased sharply due to the disturbance of the communist bandits. Only more than 400,000 yuan was collected last month, and the military expenses cannot be defaulted. How will this be remedied? (A): The situation of the shortfall in national tax revenue here is indeed as you said, and the previous second salt revenue loan needs to be repaid as agreed, which is also one of the reasons for the shortage of tax revenue. It is found that the income of the commissioner's office in June, July, August is offset, and there is a shortfall of more than 2 million yuan, all of which are related to the payment of the Central Army's expenses here. In fact, it cannot be delayed. Therefore, I came here specifically to complete this salt revenue loan to provide financial assistance. You asked how to remedy it in the future, which is indeed a current issue. However, based on my observation, the shortfall in national tax revenue due to the disturbance of the communist bandits is a temporary abnormality. Only by weighing the urgency can we find ways to divert funds to cope with it at any time. Once the military problem is resolved and the communist bandits are cleared, the tax revenue will return to its original level, and it will no longer be a problem. However, the collecting officials must be responsible for thoroughly reorganizing it. (Q): Due to the trouble of the communist bandits in various counties, Hubei local finance has been short of tax revenue for four months in May, June, July, August, and the accumulated deficit has been more than 2 million yuan. Now there is no way to divert tens of thousands of yuan. It is heard that the person in charge has been asking you for relief for days. What is the process? (A): I have already understood the current difficulties of Hubei finance. The reason is nothing more than the impact of the temporary disturbance of the communist bandits. How to find ways to relieve them is a matter related to local finance and should be handled by the competent authorities. If there are matters that should be requested from the central government in accordance with the law, as long as the principle of taking into account both the central and local governments can be followed, the Ministry of Finance will not fail to provide convenience. Zhang Xinbai, the director of the Finance Department of Hubei Province, has stated the various issues before and after, and I have replied based on this principle. (Q): It is heard that you have been soliciting customs treasury bonds from the provincial and municipal authorities. The provincial government said that the provincial treasury is empty and the local area is extremely depressed, and there is no real ability to underwrite them. What is the result of the negotiations? (A): It is found that the treasury bonds are being solicited from all provinces. I recently went to Zhenjiang and Hangzhou to visit the provincial authorities of Jiangsu and Zhejiang. It is said that they have agreed to be responsible for selling them. It must be known that the central government issues treasury bonds, which are originally required by the state. The central government's difficulties are also the difficulties of the local governments. The so-called central and local governments belong to the same body, which is the meaning of this. I have repeatedly contacted Chairman Wu and Director Zhang and Mayor Liu about this matter. At 12:00 this afternoon, I will have a small gathering with Wu and others here to make the final agreement on soliciting treasury bonds. If the province really has difficulties, I will ask the two governments of the province and the city to work together to handle it with the commissioner's office. (Q): The order to implement the abolition of transit dues is about to expire soon. In Hubei Province, the unified tax revenue is about 10 million yuan, and all local government expenses rely on its payment. If the abolition is implemented as scheduled, even if special consumption taxes and business taxes are continued to be levied, it will be enough to offset part of it, but the focus of these tax sources is in Hankou City, not within the scope of the provincial government. How will this be relieved in the future? (A): This point really needs to be considered. I believe that this kind of difficulty must be solved by the joint efforts of the province and the city. Shanghai is the essence of the whole country. If everything is considered to belong to the city, not only Jiangsu Province will feel very difficult, but the entire finance of the central government will not be able to start. Fortunately, Mayor Liu and the members of the provincial government here are very harmonious in spirit. In the future, the distribution of materials on the war front will naturally not be divided into boundaries. Everything can be discussed and handled in detail in the spirit of cooperation.

Three-Province Bandit Suppression Army Establishes Contact

Zhu, Mao, Zhang, and Huang Gather in Tonggu and Wanzai

Hunan and Jiangxi Armies Encircle Tonggu and Wanzai

(Dispatch from Nanchang) The joint suppression of Peng, Huang, Zhu, and Mao by the three provinces of Hunan, Hubei, and Jiangxi has been reported in this newspaper many times. Commander-in-Chief Lu sent Model Company signal combat planes to fly to the area of Gaoan, Shanggao, and Wanzai on the 25th to scout for traces. He reported back to the province that the main forces of Zhu, Mao, and Peng are still gathered in the area of Tonggu, Wanzai, and Xiushui, and have not fled elsewhere. There are no large communist bandits in Shanggao and Gaoan, only scattered small groups remain. According to news from the provincial government, after being severely attacked by Dai's Brigade in Xiu and Tong, Zhu and Mao retreated to the Daweshan stronghold in the border area of the three provinces. Chen Guangzhong's Brigade, the vanguard of the anti-banditry force of the Fourth Army of Hunan, has chased to the vicinity of Daweshan and is attacking Tonggu. The Xi Yi two brigades of the new 32nd Division advanced from Pingliu to Xiushui. The above two departments have established contact with the Dai Brigade of the 18th Division and are forming a large encirclement of the bandits in Tonggu and Wanzai. However, most of the bandits are hiding in the deep mountains, making it difficult to search and suppress them. Since the Changsha Incident, the central government has attached great importance to the suppression of bandits in the three provinces. Commander-in-Chief Chiang decided to send three more divisions west to be commanded by Director He after the victory of the Jinan counterattack. The two brigades of the 50th Division of the Ninth Army under Tan Daoyuan (the 150th Brigade had already returned to Jiangxi and was stationed on the Nanxun Road) have received orders to return to Jiangxi to suppress the bandits. Commander-in-Chief Lu received a telegram from Chief of Staff Zhu in Nanjing yesterday, stating, "I have just received a telegram from Commander-in-Chief Chiang ordering Tan's Division to send a brigade back to Jiangxi first on You Day, and the rest to depart one after another." After receiving the telegram, Lu has telegraphed the Adjutant's Office to prepare vehicles and ships, and prepare to welcome them. The three-province anti-banditry meeting is now scheduled to open on the 27th. The provincial government has appointed Wang Yinxi, Director of the Civil Affairs Department, and Lu Xiaochen, Director of the Security Office, as representatives to attend. The two men took the Nanxun train to Xun on the 25th and transferred to the west. (26th)

Guangzhou Arrests Communists for Days

Confessions of Yu Zuoyu and Others After Being Arrested

Military Police Also Capture Three Criminals in the Suburbs

(Dispatch from Guangzhou) The Special Investigation Section of the Guangzhou Municipal Public Security Bureau recently followed and arrested Yu Zuoyu, an important member of the Communist Party in Guangxi Province, and his accomplices Li Zhenyu, Chen Jinglu, and Ri Chang at the Shenzhen Station. Yesterday, the Public Security Bureau interrogated Yu and others. According to Yu Zuoyu, he is 30 years old, from Beiliu, Guangxi Province, a graduate of the Jiangwu Hall of the Second Training Army, and served as a platoon leader and company commander under Lin Hu. Under Li Zongren, he rose from battalion commander to regimental commander, and deputy division commander of the First Division of the Seventh Army. In October last year, Li Mingrui appointed him as the commander of the Fifth Brigade of the Guangxi Garrison. In January this year, the Central Committee of the Communist Party sent Deng Bin to Longzhou, Guangxi, to organize the Zuojiang Revolutionary Committee and the Youjiang Soviet Government. He once held a mass rally, and I also participated. In February, the Revolutionary Committee appointed him as the commander of the Eighth Army of the Communist Red Army. At that time, there were more than 600 troops, and there were also 1,700 troops in the department of Zhang Yi, commander of the Seventh Army of the Red Army. Li Mingrui was the commander-in-chief of the Red Army, stationed in Baise. He had fought three fierce battles with Huang Shaoxiong's troops. His own troops were defeated, and only more than 300 guns remained. He fled to Sile County, and the rest of the troops were commanded by Liu Guiting. After the failure, he fled from the Guangxi border to Beihai, and then went to Vietnam by sea. From Vietnam to Hong Kong, the Communist Party Provincial Committee ordered him to return to Guangxi to gather the old troops of the Red Army and join Li Mingrui's troops to go to Zhu De in Hunan. On the 17th, he was arrested at Shenzhen Station on the Guangzhou-Kowloon train. Li Zhen, whose character name is Zi, confessed that he is 23 years old, from Guiping County, Guangxi Province, and was a teacher in a Guangxi middle school. In the 16th year of the Republic, he was introduced by Hou Lizhe to join the Communist Youth League.

Page 10

He was in charge of the group leader. In October last year, he was assigned by Pan Qing, secretary of the special branch, to be responsible for the Communist student movement. He failed in Guangxi before and fled to Hong Kong last month. He was sent by the Guangdong Provincial Committee of the Communist Party to Dongjiang to participate in the work of the Special Committee. Chen Jing (i.e., Liao Guanghua) confessed that he is 26 years old, from Shangsi County, Guangxi Province. He served as an executive committee member of the Dongnan Township Farmers' Association in Shangsi County, Guangxi. In March this year, he was introduced by Nie Gen to join the Communist Party and became a member of the Agricultural Committee, organizing farmers' troops and restoring farmers' associations. In April, Red Army Commander Yu Zuoyu was chased by the militia in Matoushan, and he led the farmers' troops to rescue him from the encirclement. Later, he followed Yu Zuoyu to Hong Kong through a side road. He is now being sent to Huizhou by the Guangdong Provincial Committee of the Communist Party. Lu Richang (i.e., Wang Keqiang) confessed that he is 34 years old, from Shangsi County, Guangxi Province. He served as a member of the Agricultural Committee of Dongnan Township in Shangsi County and as a special commissioner for agricultural movement in Guangxi Province. In November last year, Yu Zuoyu appointed him as the county magistrate of Zuojiang County. In March this year, he was introduced by Nie Gen to join the Communist Party. In May, Yu Zuoyu was trapped in Matoushan, and he and Liao Guanghua led the farmers' troops to rescue him. Later, he followed Yu to Beiliu and went to Hong Kong through a side road. He is now being sent to Huizhou by the Guangdong Provincial Committee of the Communist Party, and was arrested on the way. Since the arrest of Yu and others, the anti-communist work in Guangzhou has become more rigorous. The military police have been sending detectives to investigate for days. On the 20th, they found that communists were hiding in the stone factory behind Guanyin Mountain and in Nan Village, Henan. The military police team attached Yu, platoon leader Zhang, and squad leader Zou changed their clothes and went to search. When they arrived at their destination, they saw communists Liang Ziping, Gan Lin, and Tian Yuping gathering. They suspected that the three were arrested and sent to the military police headquarters for handling. It is heard that the three men had rioted several times in Wuhua County in the 15th, 16th, and 17th years of the Republic, and fled to Nanyang afterwards. Wuhua County had purchased and arrested them. Recently, the three men thought that two years had passed, so they sneaked back to Guangzhou and made some moves. After arriving in Guangdong, they disguised themselves as workers and fortune tellers, but they were finally detected by the detective and captured in one fell swoop. (August 22)

Local dispatches

Songjiang

There is another kidnapping case in Fengjing: Cases of robbery and kidnapping by bandits in the Fengjing area are constantly emerging. Recently, it has gradually reached farmers who do not have much property, but they have also been coveted by bandits. For example, the grandson of Sun Xiangyu, a farmer in the 28th and 29th wards of Sanbao, who is only six years old, and the seven-year-old son of Zhu Jingui were both kidnapped by bandits on the night of the 29th of the abolished lunar June. It is heard that the Sun and Zhu families are not wealthy, but they have been diligent in farming over the years and have not been in debt. Now there is no news.

Petition to prohibit the opening of Hengshan: Hengyun Mountain is one of the Nine Peaks of Songjiang and has always been known as a scenic area. There is the place where Lu Yun of the Jin Dynasty studied, and there are also the ancestral tomb and ancestral hall of Zhang Zhao, a local worthy. There are many ancient tombs on it. Recently, it was heard that Wang Jisheng, in the name of Wang Hengshan, has petitioned the Department of Agriculture and Mining to collect mountain stones, and the provincial department has ordered the county to investigate and reply. Now it is learned that the descendants of the Zhang family said that although there is Wang's land on Hengyun Mountain, it is not all owned by the Wang family, and it is less than forty feet away from the Zhang family's ancestral hall, which obviously hinders the tombs of local worthies. They have appealed to the county government to forward the petition to the Department of Agriculture to prohibit it.

Kunshan

The assistant's actions are out of line: Liu Zhendong, assistant to the first district (graduate of the second session of the district chief training institute), does not work very hard on weekdays. Recently, he colluded with a villager in the eighth district to accuse Jin Deji, the district chief of the district, of bad deeds. Unexpectedly, the draft was suddenly lost and picked up by someone, who sent it to District Chief Jin. District Chief Jin believed that the accusations made by the member were all castles in the air and took a photo of the draft to report to the county government for investigation. After receiving the report, Magistrate Pang believed that the member's actions were out of line and immediately ordered his dismissal. It is heard that the district chiefs of the ten districts in the county have petitioned the provincial government for investigation.

Lake bandits wash away Jinjiazhuang: Jinjiazhuang in the county is located in the Dianpu River. Usually, residents go in and out by boat as a ferry. It is an area where lake bandits often appear. At about 10 pm on the 25th, more than ten bandit ships suddenly came to the area. More than two hundred lake bandits, fully armed, landed on the shore and went to the security team first to seize seven guns. Then they washed away the entire village. Of all the more than six hundred households, only more than thirty households were spared. When the robbery was carried out, the former manager Gu Dajun was shot and killed. At twelve o'clock, the robbery was completed. Before leaving, Gu Shande and other fourteen men and women were kidnapped and taken to the ship, whistling towards the south of Dianpu Lake. On the 26th, District Chief Zhang Zhiping of the district came to the city to report to the county for arrest. Magistrate Pang immediately ordered Police Captain Luo to lead a row of police officers to go to suppress and arrest them. At that time, the bandits had already left like the yellow crane. The village is now handling the aftermath.

Suzhou

The reactionary case is scheduled for sentencing: Ge Naibin, a communist suspect arrested by the Public Security Bureau on the 17th of last month (a teacher at Chunshen Elementary School), was publicly tried by the High Court on the morning of yesterday (27th) in the Fourth Criminal Court, with Presiding Judge Zheng Chi and Prosecutor Jin Henian presiding. After the defendant hired lawyer Song Mingxun to defend him, the judge announced that the case would be sentenced at 9:00 am on the 30th of this month.

Zhang Taijie's appeal case is scheduled for trial: The High Court has scheduled Zhang Taijie's appeal case, the former manager of the Chuanhan Railway, to open on September 13 to re-summon witnesses for the trial.

The Suzhou and Hangzhou telephones are gradually connected: The Jiangzhe telephone connection, Wu Jiang construction director Shi, to Zhejiang in general, has been connected. The test talk results are very clear. Now the section of the telephone has been scheduled to officially open on September 1. The plan is now underway to proceed from Nanxun, via Jiaxing, Tonglin, Chongde, and Chang'an, to Hangzhou. The date of success for the direct telephone connection between Suzhou and Hangzhou is not far away.

The case of dereliction of duty by the director of the Public Security Branch is scheduled for trial: The case of dereliction of duty by Zhou Dingbo, director of the Rugao County Public Security Branch, who was sentenced to one year and two months of imprisonment by the county judicial decision, was appealed to the High Court. The High Court has scheduled the trial to open on September 12.

Organize a Conscript Relief Association: Wang Dequan and other citizens of Wuxian County have initiated the organization of a Conscript Relief Association and petitioned the county government to issue a notice and passport to solicit conscripts, communicate, and transport clothes and other items. The county government has approved the application.

Strictly investigate reactionary elements: The county government recently received a secret report that a large number of reactionary elements are planning to take illegal actions in Wuxian County. After receiving the report, Magistrate Fei secretly ordered the County Public Security Bureau to conduct a strict search. Minutes of the County Government Meeting: The following matters were resolved at yesterday's county government meeting: (1) The stone archway at the north entrance of Gongxiang is obstructing traffic. The owner of the archway is still required to demolish it before September 20. If it is overdue, it will be executed on their behalf, and they are allowed to choose a site to move it. (2) The streets of the Changyuanwu three county offices are planned to be renamed, and the filled-in Xiahou Bridge is planned to be named a road. The decision will be made at the next meeting.

Changshu

A Large Number of Hunan Refugees Come to Changshu from Wuxi: A large number of Hunan refugees came to Changshu from Wuxi via Yangjian and other places. The Public Security Bureau, upon hearing the news, dispatched police to suppress them. The refugees intended to stay in the city, but the Public Security Bureau, due to recent local unrest, escorted the refugees to Ouchu Town that evening (the 25th), where they were lodged in temples and under the eaves of houses along the way. The next morning, local residents and merchants raised 40,000 copper coins to give to the refugees' representatives as travel expenses. The police escorted them to Baijie Zhitang, and then they went to Kunshan. Some traveled on foot, while others, suffering from illness, hired boats to travel by water. When the refugees left Ouchu Town, two representatives, Fang Yusheng and Tan Peng, posted a notice. The writing was not entirely coherent, but one section read: "We, the disaster victims, are from Xinhua, Hunan. We have suffered countless hardships due to repeated warfare and rampant bandits. We have been subjected to cruel torture and wanton looting. Our houses have been turned to scorched earth. Innocent lives have been sacrificed. We cannot live. Having no other recourse, we petitioned our county government for passports to beg for food in other provinces. Therefore, we lead men, women, old and young, totaling over a hundred, and pass through various places along the way, without disturbing anyone."

Police and Bandits Exchange Fire in Hupu Town: In the ancient village town, more than ten miles away from the city, four bandit boats arrived at about 2 a.m. the day before yesterday (the 26th), carrying a total of fifty or sixty bandits, all armed with guns. They entered Baiyu Weng and Ayu Estuary outside the East Gate from East Lake. They encountered a shrimp basket boat on the way in the One Family Lane near Guli Village and forcibly took the boat owner, Li Sisi, to row the boat. They then arrived at the west end of Guli Village Town, landed, and tied up Song Qian and two others nearby. The farmers in the area, hearing the alarm, beat gongs to gather the masses and sent a special messenger to report to the Security Corps headquarters. After receiving the report, the team's Second Detachment set out first to guard Ayu Estuary. Shao Junbi, the captain of the First Detachment, led platoon leader Lu Weinong and others to deploy defenses at key points in the town. A unit of armed soldiers chased to Baimao Estuary and saw several boats moving ahead. The Security Corps fired first, ordering the boats to stop. The bandit boats fired back while fleeing towards the Miaoshang Hupujiao area. However, the team members were chasing on land, and when they reached Miaoshang, they suddenly encountered a lack of water and immediately turned back. Li Songqian and the three who had been tied up were not released. After investigation, it was only known that Li Sisi was fifty years old, lived in Toutu, Forty-sixth Du, outside the South Gate, and made a living by fishing. He has a son. The Public Security Bureau has been asked to send police to rescue him.

Another report states that yesterday evening (the 26th) at about 7 p.m., the Public Security Bureau received a long-distance telephone report from Shao Qiubai, the chief of the Hupu Township Public Security Sub-Bureau, stating that a large gang of bandits, about sixty or seventy people, had arrived there and were exchanging fire with the police and Security Corps in Bixi Market (three miles from the town). After receiving the report, the headquarters dispatched Chief Inspector Lu Jinchen to gather the chiefs and police of various sub-stations, as well as the box cannon team, and took a gasoline boat to Meili Town (eighteen miles from Hupu) to set up a defense. At the same time, a special curfew was announced in the city. The reporter, hearing the news, used the telephone to inquire at a certain rice shop in Hupu Town. It was said that those who arrived were refugees and had already withdrawn from the territory. The Security Corps and others had returned to their original defenses, but the residents were still in a state of unease.

Wuxi

The Xicheng Road is Dangerous to Drive On: The southern section of the Xicheng Highway, which broke ground on April 3rd of last year, did not hold a traffic opening ceremony until the 20th of this month. The entire road is twenty-seven miles long and cost a total of over 90,000 yuan. However, the coal slag paved on the entire road is not very thick. Driving cars on the day it opened to traffic already felt dangerous. Because the road surface soil is very loose, the wheels sink into the mud and cannot move forward. Moreover, the day after the opening, there was a heavy thunderstorm day and night, and the soil felt even looser and more floating. Therefore, cars can only go to Tangtou these days. It is reported that someone has submitted a request to the Construction Department, asking for ways to provide relief to avoid public danger.

Wounded Soldiers Recovered and Left Wuxi to Return to Their Units: There are still more than 700 wounded soldiers being treated at the Twenty-second Rear Hospital stationed in Wuxi. Recently, 295 of them have recovered. President Cai sent a letter to the station requesting three cars to be prepared. Yesterday (the 27th) at about 12 noon, they took the train to Beijing and then went to the front to return to their units.

Former County Magistrate Sun Went to Japan for Inspection: Sun Zuji, the former county magistrate of this county, went to Shanghai after handing over his official seal. Admiring the development of Japanese industry and commerce, he took the Shanghai Maru steamship to set sail for Japan the day before yesterday (the 26th) for inspection.

Further Arrests in the Jiuli Base Robbery Case: The Third Sub-Bureau of the Public Security Bureau outside the South Gate previously arrested three suspects, including Yu Sanbao, in the Jiuli Base robbery case in Yangming Township. They had already been interrogated and confessed, and were being held for trial. The day before yesterday, the Eighth Sub-Bureau of the Public Security Bureau received a tip that Qian Ada, a fugitive in the case, had secretly returned to Zou. Patrol Chief Liang Desheng was dispatched to Nanqiao and arrested Qian Ada. After being brought back to the bureau, a local thug, Zhu Pangen, incited Qian's concubine to cause trouble for the Eighth Sub-Bureau. Yesterday, they were all sent to the city for trial. False Alarm of Bandits Gathering at a Garden: Yesterday, the County Public Security Bureau suddenly received a tip that more than 20 bandits were secretly gathering at Liyuan in Yangming Township, plotting wrongdoing. Director Xu, upon receiving the report, immediately dispatched Chief Inspector Qian Tianxiong to lead police officers and drive a speedboat to Liyuan. However, after searching the entire garden, nothing was found. The villagers said that they had only seen a village boat being towed by a steamship, moored in the center of the lake, with more than 20 people, both men and women, but they did not know where they had gone. After receiving the report, Chief Inspector Qian immediately searched the surrounding lakes in all directions, but found nothing. He then returned to the bureau to report back.

Zhenjiang

The County Government Closes the Zhunti Nunnery: The county party department previously received a complaint from citizens that the dirty nun Changjing of the Zhunti Nunnery and the inferior monk Mingyuan had an adulterous relationship. In February of this year, the Fifth Sub-Bureau of Public Security Bureau cracked down on the nunnery's gambling and opium den. Mingyuan escaped upon hearing the news and has not been arrested yet. The nun Changjing has not shown any signs of restraint. The case was investigated by the county party department and found to be true. The county government was notified to carry out the expulsion. It is reported that the county government sent police to close it yesterday and implemented the expulsion of the dirty nun to restore morality and maintain security.

Jiashan

The Entire Town of Taozhuang Was Robbed: At about 5 a.m. on the 26th, more than 20 bandit boats suddenly arrived in Taozhuang Town, with more than 200 bandits, speaking the Jinshan dialect, with red cloths wrapped around their left arms, all holding wooden shell guns and pistols, etc. They charged from the west of the town to the water police detachment, firing shots as a demonstration, wounding police officer Wu Xiushan. Eleven guns were robbed. They then went to the public security substation and the security corps, and the two sides exchanged fire for about two hours. The security corps was out of ammunition and was broken into by the bandits. Five members of the Security Corps, platoon leader Zou Yunfei, team members Guo Chilian, Ge Jinkui, Jiang Wen, and Wei Dewen, were killed. Patrol Officer Gao Zhiming was shot in the upper left breast and seriously injured. Ten carbines were robbed. Eight bandits were also killed. The bandits carried away the bandit corpses on the bandit boats. More than 30 shops were robbed, including Yufeng Rice Shop, with losses of more than 10,000 yuan. Afterwards, reports were sent to the county government, public security bureau, water police team, and other departments to go to suppress them, but the bandits had already fled far away.

Another piece of news states that since the bandit leader Taibao A Xu sneaked back to Jinshan, the residents of Jiashan, Pinghu, and other places in Zhejiang have been terrified. Unexpectedly, at 5:30 a.m. on the 26th, a large group of bandits, 160-170 people, with sharp guns, attacked Taozhuang in Jiashan. The town was stationed with the Fourth Detachment of the Eighth Water Police Team. After the bandits arrived in the town, they first cut the telephone lines and then surrounded the water police detachment, hoping to disarm them. The detachment and the local security corps fired at the bandits to resist. After about two hours of fierce fighting, five members of the corps and police were injured and eight bandits were killed. Because of the disparity in numbers, the official army gradually became overwhelmed. The bandits, fearing that reinforcements would arrive after a long time, also rushed to snatch several bandit corpses and fled to Fenhu. At that time, Director Xu and Hang, the commander of the bandit suppression, were riding on the Zhiguo patrol ship in the Pinghu area. After hearing the news, they led their patrol ships and wooden shell gun teams to Jiashan overnight to pursue and suppress them. After receiving a telephone report from the Jiaxing district, the Inland River Water Police Bureau also sent the Gonghe patrol ship and the Shi Dai patrol team to the lake area along Jia overnight to search and suppress them.

Nantong

The County Government Takes Over the Langshan Military Office: The Ministry of Military Affairs appointed someone to investigate and found that the old Langshan General Military Office had been occupied by the people's Horse Hai Shan and ordered the county government to take it back for safekeeping and await disposal. On the 26th, County Magistrate Zhang ordered the Public Security Bureau to take over and keep it properly.

Reorganizing the Industry Police Team in the Tai District of Taizhou: After the industry special police team in the coastal reclamation area of the Tai District of Taizhou in Huainan was disrupted by Ma Yuren colluding with bandits, most of the guns were robbed. The Police Committee has appointed someone to go to the Tai District to effectively reorganize it together with Zhang Dong, the supervisor of the Provincial Committee.

Fierce Battle Between Soldiers and Bandits in Pinghu: A large group of bandits suddenly arrived at Mashan Sanxu in Pingchao at noon on the 26th. After the riot, they set fire to houses. The provincial defense army, together with the county police team and security corps, went to suppress them. The two sides exchanged fire and fought fiercely for two hours, killing five bandits and capturing more than ten. The rest retreated westward. The Provincial Security Regiment Concentrated on Suppressing Bandits: Tongtai and other counties in Jiangbei are carrying out a large-scale suppression of bandits. Regiment Commander Li ordered Yang and Yu's battalions to concentrate in Baimu Siyu, together with the local teams, to suppress them.

Seabirds Extorted 100,000 Yuan from the Su Family: Seabirds went to the home of Su Liangqing in Liuhaisha and kidnapped eight men and women, hiding them in the bandit den in Da'an Port, extorting 100,000 yuan from Su.

Yangzhou

Hang Surname Wet Nurse Terrified the Master: Hang Yuyan, who lives in the West Street of the county, has recently been coveted by bandits for building houses and has received four threatening letters, falling from 1,500 yuan to 300 yuan. Finally, he was instructed to wrap the ocean in newspaper at 9 p.m. on the 25th and wait for collection. He was also told to put red paper on the door if he paid, and green paper if he refused. The Public Security Bureau and the Second Sub-Bureau in charge dispatched Inspector Gong Rongzhi and Patrol Officer He Ya to lead police officers to lie in ambush inside and outside the door and pretended to do as instructed. When someone arrived at the appointed time, they were chased and arrested by the bureau. They confessed their name as Zhang Fengkui (originally Yang Xiao Er Zi Ye tea shop) and were instructed by the Hang family wet nurse and the daughter-in-law of a craftsman from the Hang family to write threatening letters. It is heard that the officials have issued tickets to summon the wet nurse and the craftsman's daughter-in-law for questioning.

The Chamber of Commerce Raised More Than 4,000 Yuan: Regarding a certain zhan (merchant house) asking the Chamber of Commerce for more than 4,000 yuan, the Executive Committee of the Chamber of Commerce has now decided to reluctantly raise it. Starting from the 25th, it will be distributed to each industry according to the precedent number when Dingmao's military affairs arose.

Small Round Backwash Sunk Stone Boat: A Zhen Tai small round boat belonging to the Fuyun Company in this county brought a towboat. Yesterday (24th) at noon, it went downstream from Yang to Kai Zhen. At the same time, the Tongyu small round boat of Tiantai was placed alone in the back. When it sailed to Sanhe Yi, the Tongyu round boat planned to overtake and sail first, opening the horsepower straight forward. Suddenly, a heavily loaded stone boat came head-on. After the two small round boats sailed past, the backwash was very rapid and the stone boat was sunk. The local people detained the Tongyu round boat to handle negotiations. It was also heard that a child laborer on the stone boat had fallen into the water and drowned with the boat.

Hangzhou

The Number of People in This City: The number of people in Hangzhou City had changed again in July. The Provincial Capital Public Security Bureau has completed the investigation. There are a total of 96,558 households. The number of men is 299,490 and the number of women is 193,744. The total number of people in the city is 493,234. The number of deaths in July was 629 and the number of births was 5,788. Eleventh Principal Repayment of Post-War Public Bonds: The lottery for the eleventh principal repayment of post-war public bonds in Zhejiang Province was held last month. The Department of Finance has notified all counties to start repaying the principal from September 1st and simultaneously issue the eleventh interest payment. The Chinese Banks in the province and the county governments are the agencies for repaying the principal and paying interest.

Ordering Guns: The Zhejiang Provincial Government believes that the current situation is unstable and bandits are rampant. Although security teams have been dispatched to guard important areas, many guns have been damaged and are insufficient for deployment. The Provincial Government Meeting decided to approve 110,000 yuan and send personnel to Shanghai to order them. The Department of Finance has been collecting the funds continuously and ordered the Hangzhou Chinese Bank to remit them to Shanghai.

Educational News Sports

Preparation for the 10th World Games

To be held in the United States for 16 days starting July 30th of the year after next

The New York Provincial Government allocated 125,000 U.S. dollars for expenses

Participants from 45 countries prepare to win medals

(New York Dispatch) The 10th World Games will be held in Los Angeles, USA in 1932, as decided at the close of the 9th Congress in 1928. The Executive Committee of the Congress was held in Berlin, Germany from May 25th to 30th of this year. Representatives from 45 countries participated. After six days of detailed research and discussion on the progress of the Congress, the procedures for handling various important tasks have been drafted step by step. At the same time, the committee members also discussed the resolution of the 3rd World Winter Games, which will be held in Placid Lake in 1932.

Congress Dates and Items

The Congress is scheduled to be held from Saturday, July 30, 1932 to Sunday, August 14, a total of 16 days. The Congress items are divided into track and field, gymnastics, boxing, wrestling, swordsmanship, swimming, rowing, equestrian, cycling, weightlifting, sailing, shooting, water polo, horse polo, hockey, and tennis not included because the Davis Cup is held every year. Football may be included, but it is not yet determined because some rules require changes and will be resolved at the meeting of the International Football Association in Butte-Brassat on June 6th and 7th. Women's items include track and field, swimming, swordsmanship, and skating. As for physical performance, if it is included, it can also be listed in the order.

Tianma Ping Pong Team Wins Hong Kong Champion

Tonight at 8 o'clock Hong Kong battles the Japanese team in Shanghai

Brief Review of the Game: At the sound of the eighth bell, the Tianma players entered in an orderly fashion. The Hong Kong team players also entered, since they were living at the Jian De Club. The referee Zhou Weifen and recorder Zeng Rongzong were assigned their positions and the game began. There were more spectators than last time. Observing their skills, each had made progress. Lu Hanjun is one of the new famous generals in Shanghai, and his shot is powerful. Although Huang Jun resisted well, how could he last? The second pair was Yu Binqi against Chen Yinting. Yu is an old veteran of table tennis, and his skills are ordinary, but his experience is first-class. His hitting method is excellent. Chen is the Guangzhou individual champion, and his defeat to Yu was unexpected. The third pair was Lu Shentong against Mo Qinghuan. Lu is an athlete attending the Far East Games and is a famous general in Shanghai. His hitting method is unique, far to the opponent's table, and close to an inch over the net, making it unpredictable. Although Mo defended well, he felt overwhelmed and failed. Tianma won three pairs in a row, and the overall situation was settled. Zhou Weixin and Qian Xilin played against the illness and were unable to support themselves. Moreover, Zeng and Huo had excellent skills, so they won three to zero.

Important News

Su Chen, Director of the Department of Education, Invited Ma Yinchu to Give a Lecture

Titled "The Problem of Gold's Value Being High and Silver's Value Being Low"

Contemporary economics expert Ma Yinchu recently came to Zhenjiang as an examiner for the county magistrate examination. Chen Hexian, director of the Department of Education, believes that Ma has an absolute wealth of research on all practical economic problems. Recently, our country's society is feeling the pain of gold's value being high and silver's value being low. Ma has unique insights into this issue. Since it was a rare opportunity for Ma to stay in Zhenjiang, he specially invited Ma to give a public lecture in the auditorium of the Department of Education at 4 p.m. yesterday (the 26th). The lecture topic was "The Problem of Gold's Value Being High and Silver's Value Being Low." All sectors of society were welcome to participate. Those who came to listen to the lecture arrived in droves before 3 p.m., numbering no less than five or six hundred. Ma arrived at the Department of Education at 3:40 and entered the auditorium at 4:00. He was introduced by Director Chen, who also explained the necessity of inviting Ma to lecture on this important issue. Ma then took the stage to give a lecture, which lasted about two hours. He first described the reasons for the high value of gold and the low value of silver and their impact on China. Then, he criticized each of the relief methods proposed by various experts in recent days. Finally, he advocated using the gold standard to be consistent with the world in order to solve all problems. However, during this transition period, the gold standard is not easy to achieve. We should first adopt a virtual gold standard, that is, use silver domestically and gold externally and fix its exchange value. His words were full of vigilance, and every word was based on academic principles and in line with reality.

Situation of Losses in Hunan Educational Institutions

The Zhongshan Library Lost More Than One Million Yuan

Changsha Correspondence, the public and private losses caused by the recent intrusion, burning, looting, and killing by the Communist bandits in Hunan Province are huge. Detailed investigations are currently being conducted separately. Regarding educational institutions, the following have been verified by the Department of Education as belonging to the province: burning Zhongshan Library, Museum, Zhongshan Hall, Provincial Education Association, First Normal School Affiliated Elementary School, and destroying the Popular Education Hall, First Normal School, First Vocational School, First Middle School, Second Middle School, First Women's Vocational School, with losses of approximately several million yuan. Regarding private institutions, the following have been burned: Jianguo Law and Politics, Fuchu Middle School, Xinyi Middle School, and destroyed: Guangya, Fuxiang, Chengzhi, Guangyi, and other schools. As for other schools that were slightly damaged or suffered slight losses, there are countless others. Therefore, although the Department of Education plans to open the provincial schools on October 1, it is still difficult to determine whether they can be realized as scheduled due to lack of funds and the inability to repair the school sites. As for the private schools, if they do not open, the school sites must be stationed by the army, resulting in greater losses. They are all trying to find ways to prepare for the opening of schools, and at the same time, they are posting recruitment notices, but the tuition fees have been increased separately to make up for the losses. They have reported to the Department of Education for record. However, in order to make the Ministry of Education clearly understand the situation of the losses of the provincial educational institutions this time and the reasons for the delayed opening of each school, the Department of Education specially reported to the Ministry of Education for inspection. The text briefly states, "Unfortunately in Hunan Province, it was tragically invaded by Communist bandits in Changsha, burning and looting, and the sky and sun were dim. From July 27th, when the Communist bandits entered the city, to August 5th, when the provincial capital was recovered, it was found that the losses of all subordinate agencies and schools were no less than several million yuan. The files over the years have all been reduced to ashes. In addition, the Zhongshan Library Museum, Zhongshan Hall, and Provincial Education Association directly under its jurisdiction have all been burned without leaving any traces. Just taking the Zhongshan Library as an example, the collection of books and its plates are worth more than one million yuan. The instruments and specimens in the museum are estimated to be worth hundreds of thousands of yuan. The Popular Education Hall was only destroyed, and all the sundries, books, and printing machinery are also worth tens of thousands of yuan, which is relatively small. In addition, the Provincial First Normal School was completely destroyed, and the affiliated elementary school and the school's "part of the books, instruments, and educational supplies were burned and lost. The Provincial First Vocational School, First Middle School, Second Middle School, and First Women's Vocational School all suffered slight losses. It is fortunate that they were not destroyed." It has now been partially repaired and resumed office. Except for the Provincial First Normal School, which suffered greater losses and has a special situation that requires careful consideration, all provincial schools have to postpone the opening of school until October 1 due to tidying up the aftermath. The private schools were ordered to handle the opening of school in advance to avoid delaying their studies, and to inspect the remaining files that were burned. Fearing that only one out of ten would be obtained, all the orders issued by the Ministry of Education and the investigation forms, as well as the original copy that had been submitted, are requested to be copied separately by each department and section and submitted to the hall for compliance, so that they can be followed." (Dance)

Record of the Board Meeting of the Chinese Sociological Society

The second board meeting of the Chinese Sociological Society was held at Yipinxiang Restaurant in this city the other day. Attendees included Wu Zelin, Qian Zhenya, Wu Jingchao (representing Sun Benwen), and Sun Benwen. The following resolutions were made: 1. Regarding the urgent need to carry out various annual affairs: It was resolved that (1) the scale of the annual meeting should be slightly larger than the inaugural meeting, and the preparatory committee should formulate specific measures; (2) the annual meeting expenses should be raised through the following methods: fundraising and soliciting members, with members in various regions responsible for soliciting members between September and October to increase the society's funds. (2) Regarding raising the society's foundation funds: The following methods were resolved: (1) 5% of the fees for articles in the society's journal will be allocated as foundation funds; (2) 2% of the book price of the society's series will be allocated as foundation funds; (3) solicit donations from publishers of sociological series; (4) voluntary donations. 3. Regarding establishing essay awards and research grants: It was resolved that (1) the society will establish three essay awards for this year, with the first prize being 100 yuan, the second prize being 50 yuan, and the third prize being 20 yuan; (2) an essay award method drafting committee will be organized, and Wu Zelin, Qian Zhenya, and Ying Chengyi will be appointed as members; (3) a research grant method drafting committee will be organized, and Xu Shilian, Yang Kaidao, Tao Menghe, Wu Wenzao, and Chen Yuan will be appointed as members. 4. Regarding compiling a sociological dictionary: It was resolved that a preparatory committee for compiling a sociological dictionary will be organized, and Wu Jingchao, Hu Jianmin, and Sun Benwen will be appointed as members. 5. Regarding revising sociological translations: It was resolved that based on the "Translation of Academic Terms and Personal Names in Chinese" drafted by Sun Benwen (see Volume 1, Issue 3 of the journal), the society's editorial committee will be responsible for separately requesting experts in various fields to revise and supplement it. (6. Regarding editing the series of books: It was resolved to first contact various bookstores regarding publication matters: (1) Sun Benwen will contact the World Book Company; (2) and (3) Wu Zelin and Qian Zhenya will contact the China Book Company and the Commercial Press. 7. Regarding how to handle members who have not paid their membership fees: It was resolved that members responsible in various regions should send personnel to collect the fees. 8. It was resolved that the unresolved cases should be sent to the three absent directors, Xu Shilian, Tao Menghe, and Yang Kaidao, for ratification.

Internal Renovation, Flourishing Atmosphere

Jiangsu Provincial Songjiang Middle School completed student registration from the 25th to last night and is scheduled to open today. The newly hired faculty and staff are all well-known figures. Changfeng Painting Society

First Day of the Exhibition of Recent Works by Professors

Yesterday was the first day of the opening of the Changfeng Painting Society exhibition, and it was very crowded with visitors. New Atmosphere at Nanyang Business College

Nanyang Commercial Senior Middle School on Tongji Road has greatly expanded its scale this autumn. It has specially hired Mr. Wang Buxian, the former principal of China Middle School and a renowned author of English works in China, as the Director of Academic Affairs; Master Zheng Huixiang as the Director of the Business Department; and Accountant Xia Sunhuan as the Director of the Banking Department. The other important teachers are also well-known figures in the education field, with both academic knowledge and practical experience. The curriculum has also been improved and carefully compiled by Director Wang and the other directors to ensure that students acquire practical skills. It is also reported that the girls' department of the school (Nanyang Girls' Senior Middle School) has also undergone a major renovation. In addition to inviting Mr. Wang Buxian to serve as the Director of Academic Affairs concurrently, they have also hired Ms. Yang Nielingyu, a Master of Science from the University of Chicago in the United States, as the Director of School Affairs; Ms. Zheng Luo, a literary scholar, as the Deputy Director; and Ms. Guan Suwen, a graduate of the Physical Education Department of Jinling Women's University, as the Director of Physical Education. It is said that the school is funded by donations from overseas Chinese from Nanyang, so the foundation is very substantial. All facilities are exceptionally perfect. Therefore, the number of male and female students who have heard the news and come to study is very large. It is now scheduled to open on September 1st.

Recent News from Zhaoji Middle School

Zhaoji Middle School has been approved by the Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Education to operate as a complete middle school starting from the 19th year, and the school's name has been changed to its current name. It is reported that the school has hired Ye Tiemin as the director of the junior high school department and Lu Shiyan, a substitute bachelor from Fudan University, as a mathematics and physics teacher. The number of new students is very large, with free students accounting for one-third of them, which is a testament to the enthusiasm for education of the school's founders, Gu Yulong, Xia Defu, Zhu Wangzhi, and Zhou Zikang. It is also known that all grades of the school have vacancies and plan to continue recruiting new students.

Daxia Middle School Adds Faculty and Staff

Daxia Middle School on Jiaozhou Road is a complete middle school affiliated with Daxia University. The faculty and staff hired this term are all individuals with a strong academic background and dedication, as previously reported. It is now reported that Dr. Ding Mingquan has also been hired as the school's health instructor, Mao Yingxiong as a Chinese language and history teacher, and Zhang Jiefu as a junior high school handicraft teacher. The school's director, Master Ni Wenya, previously served as the secretary and director of the Second Section of the Municipal Bureau of Education. It is reported that Mr. Ni has formally resigned from all positions in the Education Bureau a month ago to focus on school affairs, in addition to teaching in the university department. It is also reported that the Nanjing Municipal Bureau of Education and other places have sent telegrams to invite Mr. Ni to go there, but Mr. Ni has replied with telegrams of refusal.

Faculty of Minzhi Vocational Night School

The Minzhi Vocational Night School in this city is scheduled to hold entrance exams for new students on the evening of September 4th. The school is conveniently located at the intersection of Avenue Joffre and Rue Paul Beau. It has hired Kuai Sixun (economics professor at Fudan Shizhong), Pan Mingsan (director of the Commercial Section of the Social Bureau), Song Zhuoyun (economics professor at Fudan University), Ge Yidong (director of accounting at Jiaotong University), Lin Xi (statistics at the Social Bureau), Fang Tianpei (Ph.D. in literature from the United States), and Lu Xiehua (staff member of the Social Bureau), all of whom are experts in commerce. The position of deputy principal has been filled by Lu Qingsen (Bachelor of Commerce from Fudan University), who was invited by Principal Gu Zhixing. Classes will be held after 6:30 PM, and both male and female students are welcome to enroll.

New Developments at Guangzhao Girls' School

Guangzhao Girls' Primary School on Yokohama Bridge is the only girls' school founded by overseas Chinese and has been registered with the Municipal Bureau of Education. This semester, the school's enrollment will be nearly 400. Due to the large number of new students who applied for admission, it was necessary to impose restrictions, resulting in over a hundred late applicants. It is reported that Principal Li Yunbing has further improved the school's operations, adding a research section to provide teachers and students with opportunities for study and creation. She has also hired Dr. Huang Wen, a British medical doctor, and others as school doctors to pay attention to student health. Other issues such as kindergartens and teaching have been planned by Principal Li, and the school is scheduled to open on September 1st, with classes starting the next day.

Special Feature

Thinking of the Most Effective and Economical Way for the Study Abroad Community

(Wu Xiexun)

Having traveled to various advanced countries around the world, such as the United States, England, and France, I often see that Chinese students are the most numerous. This inevitably leads to a feeling that why are there so many Chinese students in other countries, and what is their efficiency compared to students from other countries? The reason for this is simply that our government has not yet had the time to establish large-scale academic research institutions to accommodate those who have already received higher education in the country, so they have no choice but to go abroad en masse. Furthermore, due to the social emphasis on students who have studied abroad, they are inevitably driven by vanity, which reduces their efficiency in seeking knowledge. This is also what people with lofty ideals are most heartbroken about and must urgently seek to remedy. I believe that the current plan should be to have China establish its own research institutes to provide university students with research opportunities. On the other hand, given the backwardness of education and the decline of academics in our country today, research guidance must still borrow talent from foreign countries. It is still appropriate to invite foreign experts in various fields to come to China to guide research. As for the implementation methods, the money used to send students abroad can be used to invite foreign professors, so there is no need to worry about a lack of funds. Other aspects, such as the construction of school buildings, should strive for grandeur in scale, and the arrangement and equipment within the school should strive for perfection. The expenses can be sought from the return of the Boxer indemnity funds. I believe that friendly countries will be happy to comply. As for studying abroad, absolute emphasis should be placed on practical training. It would be best to change students studying abroad to practical trainees. Only after academic research is completed should the government's competent authorities negotiate with friendly countries to introduce and entrust them with practical training opportunities. This method has been implemented by our naval authorities for the purpose of cultivating naval talent. It is not only for navigation; I believe that this is the most effective and economical way to cultivate any kind of specialized technical talent. If it is absolutely necessary for the sake of facilitating practical opportunities, it may be possible to agree with various friendly countries that, for example, those built with funds returned by the United States should be used exclusively for the study of American academic disciplines, and American professors should be invited to teach them, and the United States should be asked to provide practical opportunities in the future. The same applies to England and Japan. As for whether this method has any drawbacks and whether it can be implemented, it should be decided by experts. I humbly ask the wise men of the country what they think. If you do not consider my words to be nonsensical, then please gather experts and organize a group to jointly research and implement a plan to strive for realization. At least the following benefits can be obtained: (1) The number of talents cultivated will be smaller, which can reduce the sigh of regret; (2) The talents cultivated will be more practical, which can avoid the drawbacks of pursuing vanity; (3) The ideas and academic disciplines will be more suitable for the current situation in China, so that there will be no criticism of cutting one's feet to fit the shoes; (4) Having such a large-scale, well-equipped institution of higher learning will enhance our prestige and increase our international standing. The magnitude of the benefits cannot be enumerated. As for this returned indemnity fund, there was a previous proposal to use it exclusively for transportation. Building transportation is certainly an urgent task for today, but building specialized talent to build the foundation for a new China is an urgent task within an urgent task. Our wise transportation authorities should also be willing to allocate a portion of it to complete this great plan of national construction, which will not only benefit the study abroad community. However, this matter is of great importance and cannot be effectively addressed by a junior scholar like Xiexun. It is hoped that famous figures and academic leaders in the country will jointly call for it, so that it can gradually be achieved.
