Free Talk

A Laughing Matter

— Haike

Warden (to a prisoner who has served his term and is being released): Friend, I hope you won't make trouble again this time you go out. From now on, turn over a new leaf and become a useful member of society.

Prisoner: Thank you for your kindness. I hope you do the same.

Female passenger on a boat: Boatman, what are you busy doing there? Why aren't you sailing the boat quickly?

Boatman: Miss, there's something wrong with our rudder. We need to fix it.

Female passenger: That rudder is in the water. No one can see it if it's broken. What are you so busy about?

Judge (asking a thief in his teens): Criminal, how can you be committing illegal acts at such a young age?

Thief: Your Honor, this is what you told me to do.

Judge: That's strange. How could I have told you to do it?

Thief: Because you previously sentenced my father to six months in prison. There was no food at home, so I had to take over his business. Isn't that indirectly what you told me to do?

Wife: Darling, have you forgotten that today is my birthday?

Husband: I haven't forgotten. I know you've grown another year older as soon as I look at your face.

In Memory of Martyr Li Zhongshi

— Xu Fan

Mr. Li Zhongshi was from Zhongshan. He was a stalwart member of the Nationalist Party. He was intelligent, courageous, loyal, and honest, with extraordinary boldness and insight. He followed the Premier for many years, offering counsel and assistance, and working as hard as the martyr Liao Zhongkai. Mr. Li engaged in revolutionary work with loyalty and diligence, disregarding personal gain. Therefore, Mr. Li's name has not been widely recognized. In the spring of the Xinhai year, he and comrades such as Hu Hanmin and Liao Zhongkai disguised themselves and secretly resided in Beijing. Taking advantage of an opportunity, they ambushed Zai Dun. He fought bravely alone, disregarding his own safety. However, he was outnumbered and unable to achieve his great ambition. Mr. Li was able to defend himself and leave Beijing, which was due to his extraordinary intelligence. In the autumn of the tenth year of the Republic, Mr. Li came to Shanghai on official business. At that time, an epidemic was prevalent in Shanghai. Due to overwork, he fell ill and remained in his residence. Mr. Li had always been averse to medicine. His family tried to persuade him to take it, but he refused. He sighed and said, "I have been running around for half my life, and the revolution has not yet succeeded. A great man's life and death are predestined. People eat grains. Who can avoid illness? Why rely on these herbs?" At that time, friends and relatives gathered and urged him to take Western medicine. Mr. Li firmly refused. Because of friendship, I rushed to Shanghai the next day to see him, but Mr. Li had already passed away. At that time, the warlords were in power, and the overall situation was uncertain. Therefore, he was buried in the International Cemetery. Yesterday, I passed by the side of the grave and saw Mr. Li's tomb green and lush, and I lingered there for a long time. Alas, Mr. Li died for public service, and his achievements were no less than those of other martyrs, but his heroic name has not yet been recognized. Is it that Heaven has deprived us of this talent? Or is it not yet the time for mourning? Reflecting on the past and thinking of the present, how can I not be sad? I have briefly recorded a few words to serve as an aid to revolutionary history.

Lamenting Xie Jiezi

— Jing Mengdie

The Xie brothers were both talented, and Gongzhan, Jiezi. His fame has been known in Shanghai for a long time. I had the honor of befriending him, which began in the autumn of Wuchen. When Jiezi came to Xishan to recuperate at the Meiyuan, he was actually introduced by two lyrics. In fact, we had been acquainted in spirit for several years. Before this, I had published two lyrics in Free Talk, which were works about appreciating chrysanthemums at the Lanling Chrysanthemum Society. The wise brothers saw them and praised them greatly. They recorded the manuscript and searched for the person everywhere. Therefore, when Jiezi arrived in Xishan, he was as happy as an old friend at first sight. There was a reason for this. Mr. Xishen's "Record of Autumn Boating on the Five Lakes" praised this section of writing's缘分 (yúanfèn, the concept of fate or destiny bringing people together), even comparing it to the story of Suiyuan and Hongxuelou. To me, who was at the end of my road and felt like I had found a confidant, it was no less than the knowledge of Yuzhou by the North Sea. Jiezi lived in Meiyuan for half a year, enjoying singing and poetry. He often visited or invited me for wine. We improvised sentences based on the scenery. We once compiled the works of singing and response into a book called "Taibo Yinxiao Lu". On good days in spring and autumn, he and Gongzhan repeatedly invited painters and calligraphers from Shanghai, as well as famous figures from the press, such as Li Haoran and Zhou Shoujuan, to tour Xishan in succession. The grand occasion of the feasts and singing at that time can be seen in newspaper reports. After we parted last year, we hadn't seen each other for a long time. Jiang Yun and Wei Shu were very homesick, and it was precisely because of this that Jiezi suddenly arrived this spring on the third day of the third month. Therefore, we went together to repair the禊 (xì, a ritual purification) at Meiyuan. An old friend was well, and visiting the old place again was a joy to behold. I immediately wrote an article to record this. Alas, who would have known that this reunion would be a farewell for eternity? At the beginning of the month, I was tied up in my hometown due to work. I returned to Xishan recently, and the bad news came, and I was shocked. Suddenly went to Xiuwen. I am ashamed to have failed my dead friend. The grief of death is hard to bear. Moreover, Cai Nu is still young and unable to take over her father's business. Xu Qi is writing a sacrifice to her husband. If your soul knows, it should not rest. Is there a more tragic history in the world than this? And Gongzhan's deep brotherly love, his grief can be imagined. Therefore, I wrote two poems to lament him, saying: Vaguely, the Er Lu broadcast their voices and glory. Little Xie's talent has been praised at sea. He has a special relationship with famous scholars in poetry and wine. He has spent the home of his illness in the lakes and mountains. Zhongxuan's body is weak and he is still a visitor. Changji's heart is as hard as blood and flowers. The tragic and handsome tour has become a separate world. The old rain of the Huanglu feels the end of the world. The two words "pity talent" feel the deepest. When I look back at the old friends, I feel the pain of losing my lyre. The chrysanthemum lyrics of Shuangsheng invite Qingyan. Ten thousand plum blossoms tie a vegetarian heart. Yuandu has repeatedly passed away and still cherishes parting. Once Zhong Qi leaves, there will be few confidants. The Ronghu has a guest who summons his soul. The autumn wind and snowy tears entrust the bitter song.

Strange Plants

— Shouyang

I was a guest in Chengang, near March. I came back the other day. My wife told me that her cousin Chen Binru's family had a plant growing next to the rockery in the backyard of his residence during the fourth month of the lunar calendar. It is shaped like a buttercup, about four feet high. The leaves are long and wide, with serrated edges. The color is reddish brown. Flowers bloom in the leaf axils, either purple or white, with spots on them. The petals are double and divided into seven lobes. The flowers that have bloomed and the buds that are about to bloom all hang down like trinkets. A slight breeze blows, like a light dance of colorful butterflies. However, the flower stalks have yellow whiskers and a very strong, strange fragrance. It cannot be immediately dissipated from the sense of smell. The Qi people have invited flower lovers to visit and admire it. However, none of the viewers can recognize the name of the flower. This is truly a strange plant. I have written this down to facilitate the research of plant experts in the country.

Record of the Public Banquet for the Chinese Buddhist Pilgrimage Group

— Zhao Dingming

The Chinese Buddhist Pilgrimage Group has been in Shanghai from Beijing for a little over a month. They are about to depart now. At 12:00 AM on the 24th, the Yousheng Travel Group, the Oriental Book Publishing House, and the World Buddhist Layman's Forest held a public banquet at Jueyuan on Hart Road in western Shanghai. In addition to the group leader, Tican, and the deputy group leader, Beiguan, of the Buddhist Pilgrimage Group, the attendees included the two monks Zhanran and Minghui, who had recently joined in Shanghai. Wei Juezhong, who had just come from Southeast Asia and planned to travel the world freely, and Yang Yuzhen, who had just arrived in Shanghai from India with the aim of traveling around the world, were also present. It is not easy to meet people from all over the world. Is this what is meant by having a缘份 (yúanfèn, the concept of fate or destiny bringing people together) with Buddhism? Soon after, Liu Yuqi, Song Peidao, and Ni Ruping, representatives of Yousheng, and Fafang, a representative of the Buddhist Layman's Forest, as well as guests Tian Chuqiao, Lin Liexuan, and others, arrived one after another. Then, everyone gathered under the pool heart凉亭 (liángtíng, a type of traditional Chinese pavilion usually built by the water) for a photo shoot, returned to the Great Hall of the Buddhist Association, and sat down for tea. There were fifteen guests and hosts, divided into two tables. After the vegetarian feast was served, the meeting began. (1) The three groups jointly elected Huang Jingwan to deliver a speech on behalf of the group. He said, "Buddhists in modern times are almost regarded as corrupt elements. I hope that the Buddhist group will reform with modern monks. I also hope that the group will be consistent from beginning to end and not retreat in the face of difficulties." He also cited the facts of travelers in ancient and modern times to encourage them. (2) Beiguan's reply, in addition to expressing gratitude on behalf of the group, was to describe the situation of departing from Beijing. "Our group of five set off from Beijing on July 30th and arrived in Tianjin on August 2nd. Minyan Daily and Ta Kung Pao both had the same expressions as the various newspapers in Shanghai. Minyan Daily said that our group was "a new activity of young Buddhists." Our group was extremely excited. At the same time, we want to thank all the gentlemen who supported our group. Even those who oppose our group should also be thanked, because they can increase our perseverance. We will promote and glorify Shakyamuni's compassion on this trip. We will also offer the Buddha's relics obtained in foreign countries to the Buddhist community so as not to fail the kindness of the three groups and all the gentlemen." (3) Mr. Lin Liexuan gave a speech, saying, "I am not a Buddhist, nor have I ever studied Buddhism. However, I feel that there are no real monks today. Only Tang Xuanzang in ancient times was a real monk. I have traveled all over the north and south of the Tianshan Mountains, and the icy and snowy, steep cliffs are chilling everywhere. It can be seen that it was not easy for Xuanzang to go to India alone to obtain scriptures and return to the country to translate them. And his people are worthy of admiration." He also said, "I deeply hope that the masters of the Buddhist Pilgrimage Group will" learn Buddhism on the one hand, work on the other hand, become a monk on the one hand, and enter the world to work on the other hand. We must reform Buddhism with a scientific attitude," and so on. Others such as Yang Yuzhen and Wei Juezhong also gave sincere speeches. It is a pity that the two gentlemen have been in Southeast Asia for a long time and speak Cantonese, which is not easy to understand. However, the general idea is to hope that the group will not just talk about empty words and must practice in person. They also explained the experiences and purposes of their travels. After the banquet, representatives of each group signed their names one after another. Shi Tican took out the publicity materials from Beijing to Shanghai and showed them to everyone for viewing. Among them, Master Taixu sent a letter of admonition from the summer resort in Putuo, saying, "With perseverance, take on the work of hardship, and you must persevere in order to achieve your goal. You must have real achievements before you can gain people's trust and admiration. You must not make boastful words in advance and retreat in the face of difficulties. This is essential." After viewing the materials, all the guests sighed at the group's second Buddhist purpose and hoped that they would abide by it. After signing their names, the Venerable Fafang led the guests to visit the clear, green, and quiet Jueyuan. Mr. Hu Bozhou from the East took many more photos and then everyone dispersed.

Analysis of the Recent Political Turmoil in Germany (Part 2)

— Li Liuzeng, sent from Paris

The German election campaign, which began immediately after the announcement of the dissolution of the parliament, is also an interesting study. After the Brühning cabinet dissolved the parliament, it issued a proclamation to the German people, in which it raised a question that voters should answer in the September 14 election. This question was, "In order to maintain financial order, to maintain the German economy, and to maintain all social undertakings, are the German people willing to reject the measures that the government deems necessary?" Regardless of whether the tax increase plan is necessary, people always feel the pain of tax increases. Therefore, it is difficult to predict whether the government's question will receive a satisfactory answer in the election. Moreover, the left and right wings, which are in opposition to the government, will inevitably use this question to exert their propaganda skills on the people. Reactionary parties, such as the racial party led by Hitler and the nationalist party of Xiao Zhenbai, will also take the opportunity to wait for changes and try to create a new trend favorable to their party in the desperate situation. In addition, the Communist Party will also make activities by taking advantage of the widespread unease caused by this economic change and the suffering of the majority of workers caused by unemployment. As for the Social Democratic Party, it is in a relatively superior position in front of the voters. However, it is also difficult to win a greater victory than in May 1929. The most unfavorable thing is that countless small parties, such as the Democratic Party, the Catholic Party, the Civilian Party, and the softened nationalist parties, are in the midst of the two major trends of the extreme left and the extreme right. There is a danger of being swallowed up and eliminated.

There is another noteworthy thing in the current German political situation, which is the interest of President Hindenburg in the election to be held on September 14. President Hindenburg has personally participated in the political war, such as the temporary establishment of the Brühning cabinet, the intervention in the "Iron Helmet" incident, the promulgation of the new tax law in accordance with Article 48 of the Constitution, and finally the dissolution of the parliament to maintain the Brühning cabinet, which had failed twice in the parliament. If the result of the election on September 14 is not favorable to the government, then President Hindenburg's position will be deeply difficult in the future. And to what extent will the political change unfold? No one dares to predict. What we urgently want to know now is whether the German people will turn to the left in the future, or to the right, or will they allow this chaotic political situation to continue for a while? At this time, everyone feels the pain of the death of former Foreign Minister Stresemann, which was a huge loss for Germany. After the European War, only Stresemann was able to support the precarious situation and lead the German people out of the water and fire and into the position of being comfortable.

Warmth in the Heart (264)

— Bao Tianxiao

Chapter Thirteen: Who Unintentionally Plants Fortune and Gets a Diamond Ring? Only This Fate Inspires a Song of Golden Threads

Chan Nong said, "Yesterday, I originally asked Second Young Master Zuo to come to have dinner. Today, my younger brother happened to send two baskets of crabs. Therefore, I specially asked the accountant to write an invitation and send it to your newspaper office. Did you receive it?" Zuo Shichen said, "Yes, I received it. I remember that every time lake crabs came into season, your father would personally send them over." Chan Nong said, "My father passed away three years ago. Only a stepmother is left at home, and my brother is also adopted. I am now alone and without relatives." At that time, he instructed the servant, "Auntie, go pick the crabs. Are the vinegar and ginger dishes ready?" Then he paired male and female crabs and said, "Second Young Master, have you eaten ten?" Our Yangcheng clear water crabs only have two per pound." Zuo Shichen said, "Such big crabs are impossible to eat ten of. At most, I can eat four." Chan Nong said, "Not enough, not enough... Then boil eight. The other day, I heard a guest say that there was a former Qing dynasty governor, Li Da, who could eat a hundred crabs in one go. People called him Li Hundred Crabs. His crab consumption was considered large. How come you can't even eat ten crabs?" Zuo Shichen said, "Yes, I also heard people say that Mr. Li Meian could eat a hundred crabs, and even his wife could eat twenty or so. But it was just hearsay, not seen with my own eyes, so I dared not believe it was true. Generally, at least several dozen crabs can be eaten, but it depends on the size of the crabs and cannot be generalized. Your crabs here are so big that even Li Hundred Crabs might not have such a large capacity." After a while, a large crystal plate was brought in, steaming with a large plate of bright red crabs. Zuo Shichen said to Chan Nong, "Why don't you join me?" Chan Nong said, "My stomach is not well, I dare not eat. I'll help you peel them." He also asked someone to pour a glass of brandy. While holding the crab and drinking wine, Zuo Shichen slowly asked why she came out. Chan Nong sighed and said, "As the saying goes, 'It's better to be a bird than someone else's little one.' Being someone else's concubine is never a good business. It's a long story, let me tell you slowly. Having tasted this bitterness, I am now determined not to marry." Zuo Shichen said, "What if you don't marry? I advise you to take advantage of the fact that you are not too old and marry an honest and sincere person. As the ancient poem says, 'I urge you not to begrudge your gold-embroidered garments, but to cherish your youth.' For example, even the most exquisite clothes can be easily remade if they are torn. But a person's youth is gone and never returns. Time flies, and many people waste their youth. By the time they turn around, they are already old and regretful. This means 'If you don't work hard when you are young, you will regret it when you are old.' What meaning is there in the brothel? It is precisely:

Do not greedily linger in the pleasure quarters,

Only to lament the lateness of the hour and resent the Eastern Emperor."

The Gold Market Remains Unpredictable

Advancing and retreating without any rhythm. Yesterday, the changes in the gold standard on the 27th were still hesitant, sometimes advancing and sometimes retreating, with a meandering pace. Throughout the day, there was a total fluctuation of ten taels, with a slight setback seen. The attitude of the industry was subtly panicky. As for the exchange rate, there was not much disparity, and the listed price has been reduced by half a grade. Brokers on and off the table occasionally made transactions, but without much volume. In the early market, it was initially weak, with fluctuations of three or four taels. The silver price was slightly lower and remained unaffected. Later, when buyers saw movement, the exchange rate seemed to rise, and thus it flourished. It rose sharply from 561.52 taels to 571 taels. However, investors rose one after another, and it has already been replaced. However, the market situation was still fluctuating, and trading in the late market became increasingly rare. As it was Wednesday, the exchange rate was typically sluggish, resulting in a mediocre situation. Afterwards, within 65 taels, the large bars of silver all shrank back by 3/16, and the silver price fell by 1/2.

The early market changed repeatedly. The opening gold price for October fell by three taels to 563.8 taels, and then increased from 563.3 taels to 566.5 taels, probably because of uneven trading and unstable sentiment. Later, Xin Heng and others sold, suddenly falling more than five taels, eventually dropping to 561 taels. However, it immediately rose two or three taels, and various firms eagerly bought in. Moreover, recently, British gold banks have been trading in and out, doing 7 pence 125. When the advance rate was announced, it had been reduced by 125, the US dollar was reduced by 25 cents, and the Japanese gold was increased by 75, with it then standing at 566.34 taels. However, at this time, there were still not few short positions being sold, and it has retreated to 563.5 taels. Soon, there was still broad buying interest in bank exchange rates. Markar & Co. initially bought November 7 pence 375, and later only ate in 25, and even Yuan Xing Yong, Yong Feng, etc., bought silver bars, so they immediately saw sharp profits, reaching 571 taels after 10 o'clock. Afterwards, Su Kang Run Yong Cheng Chang and others sold a lot, and the British gold seemed weak. October could be traded at 7 pence 1875, so it got worse and worse, and the sharp momentum was stimulated. Until 11:00, it was suppressed by six or seven taels, only about 564 taels. In an instant, Yuan Xing Yong, Yong Feng, etc. took the opportunity to buy in, again crossing the 570 taels mark, totaling 570.02 taels. After 11:30, selling pressure continued, unable to support it, and it plunged by as much as seven or eight taels, totaling 562.5 taels, and immediately increased to 565.45 taels. In short, the market situation was so confusing that it was impossible to speculate. The noon close was 565.3 taels, and the listed price has been changed to 630.06 taels. Japanese gold was quoted at a high of 75, and the morning price was a low of 64.5 taels, later only suppressed at 60 taels, and the noon closing was still at a low of 65.6 taels.

The late market was quiet. The afternoon opening was at 65 taels, then falling to 63.2 taels. Retailers sold, and it recovered by more than two taels, totaling 65.67 taels. After a while, it retreated to 63.34 taels. As the Indian exchange rate telegram showed growth, after 2:30, it seemed to tend towards peace, with only one or two taels of twists and turns. As it was Wednesday, there was no market for the various exchange rates, so the transactions of the various firms were also minimal. Around 4:00, it rose to 65.5 taels, then immediately retreated to 64.6 taels. The market closed at 4:30 at 64.9 taels, a drop of 1.9 taels compared to the previous day. The maximum price for the day was 71 taels, and the minimum was 61 taels, a fluctuation of 10 taels. The listed price was quoted at 66 taels, and the registered price was from 76 taels to 65 taels. The total volume of transactions before and after the morning and afternoon sessions was 76 taels. The price of goods in the early market was 63.5 taels, 64.5 taels in the afternoon, and the closing price in the afternoon was 64 taels.

Transactions were mostly fractional amounts. The transactions of the various firms were uncertain. Yu Feng Yong, Yuan Xing Yu, Zhi Feng Yong, Yuan Mao Yong, Shun Li, Wan Xing, etc. generally bought more than they sold. Da De Cheng, Yu Da, Yuan Cheng, Fu Chang, Heng Xing, etc. opened and closed, Yuan Xing Yong, Yuan Cheng Yong, and Yong Feng sold and then bought back. Yong Heng, Yong Cheng Chang, Yi Feng Yong, and Tai Kang Run all sold. In the afternoon, Yuan Mao Yong and retailers bought in, while Wan Xing, Shun Li, and Tai Kang Run all sold out. Other firms had no large transactions. The Dalian gang bought in 1,600-1,700 silver bars, and sold out 1,400-1,500. The Guangdong gang traded about 2,000 silver bars in total, roughly breaking even.

Yesterday, the HSBC listed prices for all currencies were reduced by half a grade. The British gold was reduced by 0.125, to 1 shilling 6.625 pence. The US dollar was reduced by 0.25, to 37.75 yuan. Interest Market Weakens Then Strengthens

Market Overview: The market price of foreign interest in this month has been hovering outside of 9%. Although it once reached 30%, it was a flash in the pan and disappeared instantly, and it has never fallen below 9%. The day before yesterday, it suddenly fell out of the range, and this morning it was even lower. People generally thought that it could be expected to shrink from now on. Contrary to yesterday afternoon, the sentiment suddenly showed strength, rising by 0.5%, and still reaching its original position, because the selling market was smooth again and the situation turned better. As for the trend of the silver market, the voice is very small, and it is probably difficult to expect a good situation.

Interest Dismantling Price (Foreign Interest): The morning interest rate was 7 qian 2 fen 8 li 5 hao, which was a little more than 1 hao 2 hu smaller than the previous day. The noon market suddenly rebounded to 7 qian 2 fen 9 li, because people thought that the selling market was smooth again and the situation turned around. (Silver Dismantling): The silver market is currently loose, and there is no hope of rising for a long time. It always opens at 2 fen every day. The silver dismantling is like a stereotype, but the drawing fee and listing price have been unheard of for a long time.

The Securities Exchange Will Start Trading 19-Year Cigarette Vouchers

Trading will begin on September 1st.

The Securities Exchange announced yesterday that it will start trading the current futures of the 19-year cigarette warehouse vouchers starting on September 1st. The 19-year cigarettes were issued on April 1st of this year, with a total amount of 24 million yuan, to be paid off in 36 months, with one payment of principal and interest each month. The interest rate is 8%, and the interest decreases with the principal. The futures transaction of every 10,000 yuan requires a special voucher of 800 yuan and a principal voucher of 400 yuan.

Yarn and Cotton: The Yarn Market is Still in a Stable Process

The yarn market is slightly firm, but the sentiment in the three-grade yarn market has turned weak, so some people are indifferent. The Chaozhou gang's intention to sell short is still strong. As for the buyer's attitude, it is extremely firm, and the long and short sides are in a stalemate again. Currently, the sales of yarn to the Sichuan gang are healthier. According to Japanese merchants' surveys, the bottom stock of yarn has increased again. The future trend depends on the actual needs.

The second and third sessions fell slightly, and the result was that each month rose by 3, 4, 5, and 7 cents. The Cotton Market is Gradually Coming to Life

The cotton market is stable. Due to the rebound in US cotton, the amount managed by the manager has been reduced. However, the Han gang sold 7,100 dan when the price rose, and there were also many people covering short positions, so the market situation was tighter. However, the large short position holders are still calm and have no intention of covering their positions, due to the favorable weather this year and the good production conditions of the new cotton. The price of the new cotton thrown in by various factories is 32.5 taels for the same type of fire machine cotton, which is cheaper and sent to the factories. However, foreign cotton has recently rebounded, and there are few new sellers. Retailers are buying in, and the market atmosphere is naturally returning. Subsequent steps still depend on the fluctuations of US cotton.

The Han Bidding Closing Price is Flat. In the early market of the Han Bidding, the market was firm due to foreign cotton. Rui Da and Japanese merchants covered short positions, and the market atmosphere became tighter. Each month rose by 30 cents. The opening situation in the afternoon was sharp, and each rose by 15 cents. Later, due to the large-scale sales by the Han gang, the market atmosphere was flat. The closing price was affected by the decline in the three-grade yarn and cotton in Osaka, and the selling trend was strong again, with each month falling back. The result was flat, with not much fluctuation. The total transaction volume for the day was 49,100 dan. Grains: The Rice Market in Hexia is Plummeting

Zhabei: Yesterday, the sources continued to arrive, and the market interest became more sluggish. The broken japonica rice from the North Gang was also weak by 20 cents, and the downward trend did not stop. The market form was still weak. Top-grade japonica rice was generally around 20 yuan, but high-quality goods in the Central Customs were only 19 yuan. The speed of the turnaround was unexpected. The Eastern Xin japonica rice was difficult to stand, and it was also half a yuan short, with the highest being only 17 yuan. The Southern Gang's thin indica rice also suffered a setback, and the market price hovered around 20 yuan. The source of new guest rice was becoming more prosperous, and the goods were better than before. Therefore, although it was still 13.7-8 yuan on the surface, it actually had to be discounted by 20-30 cents. The white yuan high and fixed grades were cut, and the higher market form was slightly stable, while the middle and lower grades continued to decline.

South Shanghai: A small amount of goods arrived from Hexia, and the sales were flat. The North japonica rice was facing a deteriorating situation in the North Market, and everyone was pessimistic, so the market price was observed and adjusted by 20 cents. The lower and middle grades of japonica rice from the Su Tong Gang were scarce and inquired about, so the market price had no standard. The overall trend was extremely weak. Scattered boats of thin early indica rice from the South Road were still arriving, and the route was very poor. Although the market price had been shortened, there were no buyers asking, and the transactions were minimal. The price of new japonica rice was the same as the price in the North, and the change in yuan was stable, with the overall market at 18.2-3 yuan.

The Flour Market is Falling in the Near Term and Rising in the Long Term

Yesterday, after the flour market opened, each month remained stable. The current month saw some scattered long positions return, and most of the long positions also paused slightly due to some concerns. The market was slightly flatter. The market from September onwards was inquired about by customers, and the market form was tighter. Moreover, it was widely rumored in the market that the Tianjin shipping ban had been opened due to a proper advance payment, so people were more optimistic about the distant future. The closing price was up 1.25 yuan in September, up 1 yuan in December, up 7.5 cents in October, up 0.5 cents in November, and up 0.5 cents in January. The current month was down 0.25 cents.

Wheat Futures: Bullish Momentum Gradually Softens

Morning: Determined Buying of Spot Goods Causes a Surge... Afternoon: Covert Selling Causes a Slight Decline

Yesterday, after the wheat market opened, the spot month experienced determined buying by bulls and capitulation by bears. The market seemed to gather momentum and suddenly surged to 5.29 taels per unit. Distant months, lacking new bullish drivers, remained similar to the previous day's closing. After the second session in the afternoon, some bulls were already covertly selling off several lots. Additionally, dealers from Changshu, Wuxi, and Suzhou secretly sold approximately 20 lots, immediately breaking the market's buying momentum. The spot month fell from 5.27 taels to close at 5.18 taels, a decrease of 0.03 taels compared to the previous day's close and a drop of 0.11 taels from the day's high. Distant months remained unchanged, with only September rising by 0.01 taels and January falling by 0.01 taels. The remaining months saw no change. Existing wheat factories have good demand, and bears are also buying to cover their short positions, but the arrival of goods is very limited, especially high-quality goods. As a result, over 9,000 bags were offered, and prices rose by another 0.06 to 0.07 taels.

Sugar Market: New York Sugar Suddenly Rises

Spot Raw Dutch Sugar Opens Higher by 0.05

Yesterday's sugar market communications from production areas reported the spot price of Cuban sugar remained at 1.125. New York sugar futures for September were priced at 1.11, up 0.05 from the previous communication; December at 1.24; and March and May of next year at 1.36 and 1.44 respectively, each rising sharply by 0.07. The spot price of Javanese sugar was 8.875, with September futures at 8.625 and October at 8.5625, unchanged from previous levels. In the exchange market, transactions for Dutch sugar No. 24 coarse granulated white sugar were sparse, but the market appeared quite firm. Ordinary goods were marked at 7.9 taels, high-quality goods at 7.95 taels; slightly damp sugar at 7.85 taels; No. 20 medium granulated white sugar at 7.7 taels; finely ground white sugar at 8.05 taels; the market was generally firm. Due to very limited arrivals of Japanese sugar and limited production from the Minghua factory, coupled with thin inventories, the market was lively. N-mark was priced up to 7.95 taels, with demand exceeding supply, and expectations of an increase to 8 taels in the future. J-mark at 8.15 taels also faced shortages. SH-mark rose to 7.825 taels, with a generally strong market. Minghua YRP-mark at 7.7 taels, YT-mark at 7.85 taels, and YP-mark at 7.975 taels were relatively stable. Spot medium granulated white sugar inventories were very thin. Huaxin Company opened over a thousand bags yesterday, priced at 7.6 taels, high-quality goods at 7.7 taels, with the market still appearing robust. Huaxin Company initially offered 3,000 bags of spot goods and continued to offer several hundred bags yesterday, with prices rising by 0.05 taels. Although demand was somewhat slack, the market still exhibited signs of stability.

Silk and Tea: Shanghai Factory Prices Report a Sharp Decline

Overseas Telegrams Not Relayed... Silk Sales Remain Stagnant

Yesterday, the local foreign firm silk market was lifeless. Silk mills in Europe and America are cutting production or halting operations due to economic factors, greatly reducing demand for raw silk. Although overseas silk prices have reported sharp declines, silk telegrams are still not relayed to Shanghai, resulting in a subdued market. Yesterday, Jardine Matheson only imported 10 bales of Hai Shen brand top-grade No. 13-15 strands Shanghai white factory silk, priced at 985 taels, a drop of dozens of taels. The outlook for the silk market remains pessimistic.

Wuyuan Premium Tea Exports Show Slight Movement

Yesterday, high-grade Zhen Mei tea from Wuyuan, from Baochang Yongxing and other firms, were purchased several hundred boxes due to telegrams received from foreign countries. However, the price was 110-120 taels, which is lower than before by 10-20 taels. With the oversupply of famous teas in the market, it seems difficult for the market to improve. Public expectations are for the assistance of the Russian Association, but the arrest of Russians in Hankou led to its closure. Yesterday, a telegram from the Ministry of Industry and Commerce stated that they had been released, raising hopes of reviving the Russian sales of Chinese goods.

Local News

Tomorrow Morning Citizens' Assembly

Eliminate Communism and Suppress Rebellion, Celebrate Victory

Citizens of this city, because the Central Army has recovered Jinan and the suppression of rebellion is achieving successive victories, and the three rebellious figures of Yan, Feng, and Wang are about to be eliminated, there is a real need for celebration. At the same time, because the three rebels instigated the Communist Party to commit murder and arson in Hunan and Jiangxi provinces, resulting in an unprecedentedly tragic catastrophe,

Suppress Rebellion and Eliminate Communism, Celebrate Victory

At a time when the National Revolutionary Army unified the country and the central government was preparing to begin political tutelage, the rebellion of the Yan and Feng warlords suddenly occurred. This is truly a matter that makes our hearts ache. Since their rebellion, the people of the Northwest have been plunged into dire straits and immense suffering. Since their rebellion, the whole country has been in turmoil, and our work of political tutelage has been unable to proceed. They are the sinners of the Party and the nation. They are a group of demons in the revolutionary process. If we want to establish the Party and the nation on a bedrock of security and prevent the revolutionary cause from being abandoned halfway, we must first eliminate them, especially their ringleaders, the instigators of this rebellion: the three rebels, Yan Xishan, Feng Yuxiang, and Wang Jingwei. These three people are colluding with each other, and their doctrine is one of betraying the Party and harming the country. Although they say "courtesy, courtesy" with their mouths, they are only engaging in clever plundering and selling out the Party and the nation. Although they are shouting "all benefits belong to the people" all day long, in reality, exorbitant taxes and levies are as numerous as the hairs on an ox. The compatriots under their rule dare to be angry but dare not speak out. They are all eagerly hoping for the arrival of our Central Army. Recently, they have organized a so-called expanded conference with absurd statements and bizarre actions. Under the guise of revolution, they are actually selling out the country and the Party. The baseness of their character and the filthiness of their methods have reached an extreme. To summarize their crimes,

It is difficult to exhaust them all. Compatriots, "to catch bandits, first catch the king." They, the three of them, are the instigators of this rebellion, the ringleaders of the rebel army in the Northwest. If there were not these three madmen with no sense of shame, this rebellion would never have broken out. Therefore, we should, day and night, spare no effort to first suppress these three. In the past, there was a man in the Jin Dynasty named Zhou Chu who once eliminated three scourges. We should now rise up and eradicate the three scourges in the revolutionary process. In addition to suppressing the rebellion, our second step now is to eliminate communism. Everyone knows that communism is not suitable for China. Because China currently has no large bourgeoisie and is an industrially backward country, there is no possibility of implementing communism at all. However, there are now many blindly optimistic young people who have not recognized this point and are blindly shouting and running around with the Soviet government, which has no homeland. They take money from their masters and come to their own country to desperately stir up trouble, run magazines, and distribute leaflets, stopping at nothing in the hope of confusing the public, especially the young workers and peasants, so that they will rise up and engage in the work of destroying the Party and the nation and slaughtering the people. Recently, they have intensified their efforts and taken advantage of the Party's suppression of the rebels to carry out riots. The recent rebellion in Changsha and the exposure of the conspiracy of Xiong Guohua, the communist member of the Nanchang Social Affairs Bureau, are very obvious examples. If this continues, the danger is immense, and the future is chilling. Compatriots, rise up! Think of the future of the Party and the nation, think of your own happiness, you can no longer compromise with them. If your blood has not yet cooled, if you are willing to be a man of passion, you should rise up without hesitation to eliminate them, "banish them to the four barbarians, and do not share China with them." Demons will eventually be destroyed when they encounter sunlight. Icebergs will eventually melt in the spring. Armies with doctrine will eventually sing "songs of triumph" when they encounter a rabble. Now our upright banner, the just and righteous revolutionary army, is already preparing to enter the gate of triumph. According to recent reliable news, Tai'an has already been recovered, the enemy army in Jinan has been almost completely eliminated, and the communist party in Changsha has already fled far away upon hearing the news. At the same time, the Jinpu Line and the Longhai Line have also achieved great victories. The expanded conference that caused a sensation for a time has now reached a period of decline. Internal conflicts among the rebels are even more intense. The three rebels, Yan, Feng, and Wang, are all dreaming different dreams and clinging to their own opinions. Their collapse is not a problem. Their own graves have long been dug and are ready to be buried. In this sweltering summer, the brave soldiers at the front are desperately killing the enemy. Compatriots, we in the rear should unite and act as their support. Rise up, let us shout:

Down with Wang Jingwei, who betrays the Party and harms the country! Down with Yan Xishan, who indulges in cruelty towards the people! Down with Feng Yuxiang, who sells out the country and harms the people! Eliminate the Chinese Communist Party, which kills and sets fires! The Chinese Communist Party is the only enemy of the people! Eliminate the Chinese Communist Party, which deceives workers and peasants and slaughters the people! Console the meritorious suppression-of-rebellion soldiers who are toiling hard at the front! Celebrate the victory of the suppression-of-rebellion soldiers at the front! Long live the Chinese Nationalist Party! Long live the success of the National Revolution! Long live the Republic of China!

The Propaganda Department of the Special Municipal Committee of the Chinese Nationalist Party in Shanghai

The spirit of the whole city is exceptionally indignant. Therefore, the preparation for the citizens' assembly is to show the determination to eliminate communism and celebrate the victory in suppressing the rebellion, which has been recorded in yesterday's newspaper. Now all the matters of the conference have been prepared. The details are as follows:

Notice to all sectors. The Shanghai Special Municipal Executive Committee of the Chinese Nationalist Party yesterday notified all sectors, stating that since the rebellion of Yan and Feng and the central government's attack, successive victories have been achieved. Recently, Jinan was recovered, and most of the rebellious enemies collapsed. The period for resolution should not be far away. The committee has decided to hold a "Citizens' Assembly to Eliminate Communism and Celebrate Victory in Suppressing Rebellion" at the public sports field in the South City at 9 a.m. on August 29th. All organs, schools, and mass organizations in this city, as well as all party members and citizens in the city, should participate uniformly. In addition to sending letters separately, this notice is hereby given.

Participation Guidelines: (1) All workers, students, party members, and citizens in the city must participate in the citizens' assembly. (2) To participate in the citizens' assembly, you must obtain symbols, flags, and slogans from the Citizens' Training Association. (3) Those who have not obtained flags and slogans from the Citizens' Training Association must each prepare a flag. (4) The wording of the flags and slogans is stipulated as follows: 1. Support Commander-in-Chief Chiang, who has made great contributions. 2. Down with Wang Jingwei, Yan Xishan, and Feng Yuxiang, who collude with the Communist Party to harm the country and the people. 3. Eliminate the Chinese Communist Party, which kills and sets fires. 4. Celebrate the victory in the recovery of Jinan. 5. The victory in Jinan is the victory of the Three Principles of the People. 6. Long live the Chinese Nationalist Party. (5) Citizens participating in the assembly must gather at the public sports field before 9 a.m. Do not be late or leave early. (6) Citizens participating in the citizens' assembly must not privately bring propaganda materials and distribute them inside or outside the venue without the permission of the Citizens' Training Association. (7) Citizens participating in the citizens' assembly must absolutely obey the command of the commander-in-chief and the chief inspector and the inspectors.

Yesterday

Defense of the South City Intensified

Yesterday, the defense of the South City of this city was suddenly intensified from 2 p.m. yesterday. Municipal public security police wearing pistols were temporarily stationed at Ximen and along the Republic Road and Zhaozhou Road on the border between the Chinese and French concessions. It is said that the reason is that in view of the current unstable situation and rampant bandits, there is deep concern that villains will mix in and cause disturbances, especially in the areas adjacent to the Chinese and French concessions, which are prone to diplomatic disputes. Therefore, today, the defense of the North and South cities of this city should be slightly intensified at any time to consolidate local security.

Resolution of the Sino-German Aviation Agreement

Statement by Wang Xiaolai, Standing Committee Member of the Silk Industry

The Issue of Japanese Cocoons Coming to China

Existing cocoons are insufficient for the raw silk materials needed in Jiangsu and Zhejiang

However, the suggestion to use Japanese cocoons is unlikely to materialize

The arrival of Japanese cocoons in China has a significant impact on our country's sericulture industry, which has attracted the attention of industrialists. The Municipal Chamber of Commerce has also received a proposal from Gu Suming, a member of the Jiaxing Chamber of Commerce, advocating for measures to prevent it. The chamber will submit it to the Standing Committee for discussion. Yesterday, a reporter from the New Voice News Agency specifically visited Wang Xiaolai, chairman of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce and Standing Committee Member of the Silk Industry Association, to inquire about the truth of the matter. According to Mr. Wang's statement, China is a country based on agriculture, and the benefits of sericulture are also well-known. However, this year, both rice harvests and cocoon production have been poor. It is a pity that our country has always paid little attention to statistics, so it has not been able to provide accurate figures on the total national cocoon production and the amount of cocoons required by silk factories. Therefore, there is no way to adjust and prevent it in advance, and there is concern of digging a well only when thirsty when the time comes. In fact, cocoon production statistics are not very difficult. Even based on the cocoon tax collected by the government, a rough estimate can be obtained. Silk factories can be instructed to have the General Association of Silk Factories in Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Anhui provinces report. In this way, if Chinese cocoons are sufficient for domestic factory use and there is a surplus, they can still be exported abroad. If they are only sufficient or even lacking, exports can be prohibited, or the cause of the shortage can be investigated and remedies sought. This spring, Japanese silk merchants also came to China to purchase cocoons for shipment to Japan, about 2,000 piculs. As for the current stock of cocoons, statistics from the number of reeling machines in Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces, including remaining cocoons, are still insufficient to supply the raw materials for silk reeling for one year. Taking Shanghai as an example, there are currently 108 silk factories, with a total of over 100,000 workers. If production stops due to a lack of cocoons, the livelihoods of the workers will inevitably be affected. Therefore, manufacturers have proposed purchasing Japanese cocoons. However, this proposal has not yet materialized. There are three reasons: (1) The value of Japanese cocoons is 200 Japanese yen per picul. The current Japanese exchange rate is high, equivalent to about 300 silver taels. Adding in the loss from silk reeling, the best cocoons yield 300 catties, and the next best yield 400 catties. Based on this calculation, the cocoon price is already 1,200 taels. Adding the reeling labor cost of 100-200 taels makes the cost too high, and silk factories may even worry about losses. (2) Japanese cocoons must be steamed with a cocoon boiling machine to be suitable for use, but very few Chinese silk factories have this equipment, only about one-tenth of the total number of silk factories. Therefore, different machinery cannot be used together. (3) Silk threads with a count of 13-15 or below are considered fine silk, and those with a count of 13-15 or above are considered coarse silk. Japanese cocoons can only be reeled to a count of 16-18, which cannot reach 13-15, let alone below 13-15. Due to the above three reasons, the proposal to purchase Japanese cocoons was eventually shelved. Except for a few dozen catties of sample cocoons shipped to Shanghai, there were no large-scale imports. Previous reports that a certain Japanese ship transported several packages were found to be untrue. However, the fact that Chinese people pay attention to this is a good phenomenon in the industrial sector. If our country can actively promote agricultural products and increase production, not only will Japanese cocoons not be able to enter, but American wheat, Indian cotton, and Saigon rice can also be expected to disappear, etc.

The Future Does Not Look Optimistic

The French Arbitrator Has a Very Firm Attitude

Their Demands Exceed the Scope of Arbitration

As a result of the negotiations in recent days regarding the China Merchants Bureau Jinliyuan Wharf case, although the French Consul-General Gankerlin has expressed a very good attitude, the arbitrator from the San De Tang (a French organization), Yaminer, has a very firm attitude and wants to insist on implementing the contract termination, which is completely against the original intention of arbitration. Yesterday, a reporter from the New Voice News Agency obtained accurate information from a certain source and recorded it as follows:

Yaminer's Opinion: San De Tang Decided to Arbitrate

After becoming the arbitrator, our arbitrator Gao Shuo, a lawyer, immediately visited Yaminer. According to Yaminer's statement, he still cannot deviate from legal solutions and requested that Gao Shuo draft a written opinion to be sent to the French Public Office. Gao Shuo agreed to consider it and immediately requested that Yaminer first submit his written opinion for review. It is now heard that it was sent to Gao Shuo's residence on the evening of the 25th. According to his opinion, there are three points: (1) Deposit 12,000 taels of rent received by San De Tang from the China Merchants Bureau for the spring and summer seasons. (2) Limit the China Merchants Bureau to return the wharf and real estate buildings by the end of August of this year. (3) Subsidize the China Merchants Bureau with 6,000 taels for the old materials used in the warehouse. He completely regards himself as an arbitrator who implements the contract termination method.

Gao Shuo Visits Gan: After Receiving Yami

ner's written opinion, Gao Shuo, a lawyer, believed that it completely violated the will of the French Consul-General and decided to visit Consul-General Gan again this morning for active negotiations in preparation for arbitration.

Original Contract Stipulation: In 1916, Article 11 of the contract renewal between the China Merchants Bureau and

San De Tang stated: "If there is any dispute between the two parties regarding the interpretation and performance of this contract, it shall be submitted to two arbitrators, one selected by each party. If there is any dispute between the arbitrators, the two arbitrators shall select a third arbitrator who has the full power to adjudicate and bind both parties, and no further request shall be made to the court for reconsideration. The arbitration fee shall be borne by the losing party."

Jiangsu and Zhejiang Silk Weaving Association

Telegraphs to Request Exemption from New Silk Tax

The Jiangsu and Zhejiang Silk Weaving Association telegraphed the Executive Yuan and the Ministry of Finance of the National Government yesterday, requesting exemption from silk and satin donations and taxes after the abolition of Likin. The original text reads, "Our association recently received a telegram from the Ministry of Finance on July 29th, presenting the Minister of Finance with deep affection and remote encouragement. Our association members are deeply grateful and have notified all silk industry groups in Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces to respectfully comply, work hard to improve, increase the sales of Chinese silk, expand production, and live up to the virtue of the kindness and benefit the people. However, our industry members have suffered from the proliferation of donations and taxes for a long time. We are rejected by other countries with heavy taxes and plagued by heavy and harsh taxes in various places. Like sheep butting a fence, we are in a dilemma and can hardly move forward or backward. Every time we pass through a place, we have to pay another tax, so we cannot sell far away, and those who are not on the verge of extinction are few. Fortunately, you have a clear understanding of the crux of the problem and resolutely plan to implement the reduction and exemption of silk and satin donations and taxes when abolishing Likin to save the industry from danger. We are grateful for your great virtue and benevolence. Now, the temporary plenary meeting of the industry in Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces has resolved and telegraphed to the Ministry of Finance, requesting that when Likin is abolished, no new donations and taxes of any kind in the name of offsetting should be allowed to occur, so as to obtain fundamental relief, etc. It is reasonable to follow the resolution and present a special telegram. I hope that you will graciously approve and resolutely preside over it, which is no different from bringing the dead back to life, and it is also the honor of our industry alone. We directly present it, and we ask for instructions to follow. The national economy and people's livelihood depend on it for survival, which is a great convenience. Jiangsu and Zhejiang Silk Weaving Association bows and kisses the seal."

Yao Cong Discusses Japanese Police Administration

According to the National News Agency, Yao Cong, the former director of the Capital Police Department, was appointed by the National Government as a special commissioner for inspecting Japanese police administration this spring. He returned to the country from Japan a few days ago and will go to the front line soon to visit Chairman Chiang and present everything in person. Yesterday morning, a reporter from the National News Agency specifically visited Yao at his residence in Yipinxian to inquire in detail about the current situation of Japanese police. According to Yao, Japanese police administration has four major characteristics: (1) Organization. The Japanese police organization is consistent throughout the country, unlike the police in the United Kingdom and the United States, some of which belong to local organizations and some to the central government, with different treatments and different degrees of work. Therefore, Japan is quite proud of its unified police administration. With unified police administration, it can achieve unified command under the orders of the Ministry of Interior. (2) Power. Japanese police were once subordinate to the Ministry of Justice and the Ministry of Military Affairs, but police administration did not improve. Since the Meiji Restoration, police administration has become independent and has made progress day by day. Recently, even soldiers who commit crimes can be arrested, but they must be handed over to the military police for punishment, and the military police must also punish them according to law. Therefore, soldiers not only dare not bully the police, but also have considerable respect for them. There is no hindrance to the exercise of police power over the people. (3) Education. Most of the current Japanese police have graduated from middle school, followed by graduates from specialized schools and elementary school students, and there are also university graduates. With excellent qualities, they are also given police education, so they can be responsible for maintaining safety. (4) Treatment. Japanese police are all officials. Even those who are on the streets responsible for guarding and directing traffic are treated as appointees, not as soldiers like in our country. After 15 years of service, they can apply for retirement, and the annual retirement allowance is one-third of their original salary. Because of the good treatment, it can attract outstanding people and enable them to devote themselves to their work and not abuse their political lives. (5) Funding. Taking the Tokyo Metropolitan Police Department as an example, the annual budget is more than 18 million. The national inspectors are subsidized by the national government, totaling more than 80 million, and several times more is paid by local taxes. With more funding, it is easy to do things. Looking back at the Capital Police Department in our country, it only had more than 1 million per year when it first started, which is really incomparable. Furthermore, Yao has detailed records of this inspection and has written "Record of Japanese Police Administration Inspection," which has been completed and will be published next month.

New Developments in Coastal Shipping

Wenzhou Adds New Ships: The Shanghai-Wenzhou route is listed as an inland航线 (hángxiàn, shipping route). When the three companies signed the shipping contract, foreign merchants were prohibited from operating steamships. This year, the shipping industry in the port has gradually improved due to the transportation of a large amount of tax grain. There are currently two steamships and four motorboats operating on Shanghai. The Zhejiang Construction Department has agreed to open the Wenzhou commercial port and dredge the Ou River to develop Zhejiang's sea transport wheel (sea vessel) industry. An on-site survey and plan are already underway. In order to expand the Zhejiang sea route shipping industry, the Sanbei Company in this port has specially ordered a 1,000-ton sea vessel at its factory, named Sanbei, which is preparing to open the Shanghai-Wenzhou route. The hull is now ready and can be completed within three months. This wheel (vessel) can start operating in the early winter of this year.

Foreign Cloth Transport to Ningbo Greatly Reduced: Ningbo's increase in the import tax on foreign cloth caused opposition from the Pitou (bulk cloth) industry in Shanghai. Initially, it was proposed to increase the Pitou (bulk cloth) tax by 400,000 yuan per year. Then, the tax bureau changed the method to collect 7 jiao (a unit of money) for each piece of foreign cloth. After the announcement of this matter, the Pitou (bulk cloth) industry in Shanghai adopted a passive boycott, stopping the shipment of a large number of Pitou (bulk cloth). Those that had to be transported were changed to added boxes and taken away as passengers and goods so that they would not be considered pieces and could be exempt from taxes. As a result, the export goods of the four companies on the Shanghai-Ningbo route suddenly decreased. This matter has not yet been resolved.

Mediating the Chongming-Hai'an Tide Dispute: The six wheel (sea vessel) companies in the Chongming-Hai'an route, such as Shanghai Ping'an and Daxing, suffered significant losses as a result of competing for business and indiscriminately dropping passenger fares. Last time, the Shanghai Shipping Association invited the six companies to mediate, advocating unity and cooperation. After the agreement was reached, disputes arose over the allocation of annual operating quotas, leading to a breakdown. The companies then submitted a request to the ministry for assistance. The ministry has already replied and sent a letter to the Shanghai Shipping Association, instructing it to send committee members again to mediate with the six companies on behalf of the ministry to resolve the dispute as soon as possible and avoid mutual destruction. The companies have been notified to send representatives to the meeting to discuss the method of reconciliation so as to avoid mutual injury.

Yuanda Ship Released by Soviet Russia

Yutong Acknowledges and Pays 57,000 Yuan in Towing and Repair Costs

Yutong Company's Yuanda ship was chartered by the Soviet Russian Commercial Fleet last time. Because it ran aground in the middle, it was towed out by a Russian ship. Afterwards, it demanded 92,000 yuan in towing and rescue costs and repair costs and detained the Yuanda ship. Chen Xietang, the owner of Yutong, negotiated with the Soviet Russian fleet repeatedly, but there was no outcome. Later, after the British merchant, Maler, the owner of the Shangci 洋行 (foreign firm), mediated, the towing and rescue costs and repair costs were purchased from 92,000 yuan to 57,000 yuan. This matter was finally resolved. The payment was remitted by Yutong from the 朝鲜银行 (Chosun Bank). The Soviet Russian Commercial Team has already received it and will release the Yuanda ship. Because the Shangci 洋行 (foreign firm) has a large amount of Russian timber loaded in Vladivostok, it ordered the Yuanda ship to transport the Russian timber to Shanghai. The case of the Soviet Russian detention of Chinese ships has come to an end.

Therefore, yesterday, it requested assistance from the Joint Association of Trade Unions in the cotton mill industry. The letter has been sent.

Explanation of the Resignation of Association Staff

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce sent a circular to various trade associations to explain the regulations on the resignation of staff from various trade associations, stating: "Dear Sirs, in the past, this city has inquired from various colleagues about the resignation of association staff due to certain matters. Whether this authority belongs to the party headquarters, please forward it for explanation, etc. After reporting the situation, the Social Affairs Bureau indicated that it was still on record. Now, on the 25th of this month, the Social Affairs Bureau approved the reply, stating, 'The report is known. In addition to the provisions of Article 8 of the Commercial and Industrial Associations Law, merchants who are not members or representatives of trade associations, and in the recent Revised People's Organization Organization Plan, Section 3, Article 3, Item 5, there are provisions that those who have counter-revolutionary actions or have been deprived of public rights or expelled from the party shall not be members. Those who have been expelled from the party shall not be members of the organization, and of course, they shall not be members of the association. As for the right to limit the dismissal of members of trade associations, it has been clearly stipulated in Article 22, Paragraph 3 of the Commercial Association Law, which shall be applied to the trade association. Please be informed, etc., has been received by the association. Inquiring Article 22, paragraph 3 of the Commercial Association Law, the regulations on the resignation of officials state that "If the officials violate laws and regulations in their duties, engage in private fraud or other major improper behavior, they shall be ordered to resign by the members' congress, or they shall be ordered to resign by the Ministry of Industry and Commerce or the highest local administrative agency," Now, for the foregoing reasons, the resignation of trade association staff shall be governed by the foregoing regulations. The text of the article is recorded immediately. Please check and handle it accordingly."

Lawsuit Regarding Eviction from Yongkang Lane

Tenant Accuses Landlord

The landlord of Yongkang Lane on North Sichuan Road, last month, entrusted a lawyer to send letters to all tenants, stating that the property had been sold by Yongkang Company to Wanfu Company, and that the house was planned to be demolished and rebuilt. Therefore, all tenants were required to move out by August 15th. After receiving the letters, the tenants were greatly alarmed. It was discovered that the company (Yongkang Company) originally had seven or eight shareholders who jointly established it. In June of this year, two or three of the shareholders invested in a merger and renamed it Wanfu Company. They were falsely using the name of demolition and reconstruction to drive away tenants, and then renovate the premises to freely increase rent. The house was built on land leased from the Yao family in the second year of the Republic of China (1913), with a term of twenty years. Counting to the present, there are only three years and several months remaining. There is no reason for demolition and reconstruction. Therefore, all tenants (a total of fifty-six households, large and small, with more than seven hundred people) besides moving out, actually have forty-eight households. They publicly elected representatives Zheng Guogan, Ouyang Hengran, etc., and also hired lawyer Chen Wenxiang to file a petition with the District Court, requesting an injunction to prevent unwarranted eviction, in order to maintain people's livelihoods. The case had a hearing once, and was not concluded. The day before yesterday morning, presiding judge Zhao Zhenhai held another hearing. Many people attended the hearing, as many as sixty or seventy people, mostly tenants from the lane. The visitors' seats were full. On the defendant's side, lawyer Tao Jiachun was retained to make a statement in court. After the judge took his seat, he asked the plaintiff's lawyer what he was requesting. Lawyer Chen stood up and said, "I request the court to order the defendant to prevent the plaintiff from moving, and to not increase the rent." The defendant's lawyer stood up and argued, "It is found that each tenant owes rent for ten months or eight months. Under such circumstances, moving is unavoidable." The plaintiff's lawyer stood up again and said, "Most of the tenants are brokers, and moving is very difficult for them. I request the court to help them." The judge then instructed the two lawyers to reconcile outside the court. If reconciliation fails, another hearing will be held and a judgment will be made according to the law.

Rice Boat Damaged by Reckless Boat

Two Crew Members Missing

Heavy Losses

The rice selling boat Taifusheng, recently collected 180 shi of white rice from Ye Jin area in Songjiang, and transported it to Shanghai for sale. The day before yesterday morning, while sailing on the Huangpu River in front of Dujia Hang, it was suddenly struck by a reckless foreign steamship traveling at high speed. Tao saw it and was steering to avoid it, but the right side was violently struck by the steamship. There was a hole more than a foot in size. Three of Tao's crew members were knocked into the water at the time. The steamship, seeing the accident, continued to speed away. Fortunately, a customs patrol boat saw it and stopped it and brought it back to help rescue. One of Tao's crew members was rescued by the customs patrol boat. Two other crew members are missing. Tao's boat was flooded and was about to sink. The steamship arranged for it to be towed to the beach. However, the rice in the cabin was all wet. He negotiated with the steamship to compensate for the loss of the boat and cargo. At first, the steamship did not admit responsibility, but later agreed to compensate 300 yuan for the damage and repair of the boat. Tao refused, because the rice was all wet, and the loss was considerable. He continued to pursue the steamship. The ship has been detained and negotiations are underway. It is unknown how it will end.

Collision of Boats Leads to Drowning of Young Girl

Sun Xianji Refuses to Give Up

Sun Xianji, from Yandi, is over forty years old. His wife, Zhou, has three sons and a daughter. He makes a living by rowing a boat. Yesterday afternoon, around 4:00 PM, Sun's boat was docked in front of Yongsheng Lane on Wuzhen Road Bridge. At that time, Chen Laohai, a Haizhou native, was steering his cargo ship, intending to set sail. Unexpectedly, in a hurry, he violently bumped Sun's boat. Sun's eight-year-old daughter, Sanbao, was standing in the front cabin of the boat, lost her footing, and fell into the river, drowning immediately. Although Sun called for many people to try their best to retrieve her, they were unable to do so. He arrested Chen and his assistant Shi Youming and took them to the Second Division of the Zhabei Water Patrol for investigation. As the case involved human life, they were instructed to send the plaintiff and defendant together to the judicial section for review.

Brick Boat Sunk to the Bottom of the River After Being Struck

Sailboat owner Zhou A'mei, the day before yesterday, in the Fengjing area, loaded 21,000 bricks purchased by Lunji Brick Store on Xinzha Road in Shanghai, and sailed to Shanghai. At around 7:00 PM that night, when she arrived at the Dongjiadu riverfront in Nanshi, a Jiangnan Datug boat from the Jiangnan Shipyard suddenly sped from the north. The tugboat saw the boat in front and immediately tried to avoid it. However, the pile driver boat was large and clumsy, and could not avoid it in time, causing the brick boat and its cargo to be completely sunk to the bottom of the river. Fortunately, all seven people on board were rescued. It is reported that the loss of the boat and cargo totaled more than 4,000 yuan.

Three Bullets in Leg After Dog Race

Wu Zhicheng Encountered Violence En Route

Wu Zhicheng, a native of Jiangdu, is thirty-two years old and has been doing business in Shanghai for many years. He previously opened the Hongkou Lianji Transportation Company in Hongkou. Two days ago, he moved to a new house at No. 46, Garden Lane, Lane 129, Jin Shenfu Road in the French Concession. Wu himself is the second landlord. There is only his wife, Shi, in the house. Wu is fond of gambling. Horse racing in various parts of Shanghai always draws him to it. Recently, with the rise of dog racing, Wu has become an even bigger dog enthusiast. The night before last was the date of the Yiyuan dog race. Jin Shenfu Road was nearby. He went there happily. It wasn't until 12:15 yesterday morning that he finished the race and returned. Unexpectedly, as soon as he arrived at the entrance of the alley, two people in white shirts and trousers standing by the side of the road saw Wu coming and greeted him. Wu stopped. One person approached and whispered to Wu, "Please help me today." Before Wu could answer, the person took out a pistol from his sleeve and fired at Wu. Fortunately, he did not hit him. The bullet hit the wooden door of the Qiankun Tai grocery store at No. 127 at the entrance of the alley and made a hole in a kerosene tin can. Fortunately, the can was empty, so no disaster occurred. Seeing that one shot missed, the assailant aimed at Wu's lower body and fired three shots in a row. All three shots hit the upper part of his left leg. Wu screamed for help. When neighbors arrived, the assailant had already fled without a trace. People reported it to the police. The police chief, upon hearing the news, immediately ordered the detective to investigate and sent Wu by car to the nearby Guangci Hospital for treatment. According to the doctor, none of the three bullets hit vital points. His life could be saved. But a part of his tibia has been injured.

Unexplained Death of a Woman

Xu Baoju, Alone and Without Family

Unknown Poison Used for Suicide

Xu Baoju, a twenty-three-year-old woman from Hangzhou, lived alone in No. 24 Pingwang Street. No one knew her background. The waiter Chen A'dong went to her room to call her to answer the phone. Unexpectedly, the woman had already secretly taken poison and committed suicide. He immediately reported it to the Laoza Police Station, which sent detectives to investigate. The cause of death was not clear. The body was taken to the Feilun Road morgue. First, a doctor from the Public Works Department examined it. The result was that it was difficult to determine what poison she had taken. It was speculated that she might have swallowed opium. Yesterday morning, Guo, a prosecutor from the Special District Court, was commissioned to inspect the site. Although the police summoned the neighbor, Mrs. Yang Qu, they were unable to find out what kind of person the woman was or the cause of her death. Since no family members were found, Guo ordered the Pushan Villa to provide a coffin and burial. He also ordered the police to investigate the cause of death and report it for verification.

Electric Fan Kills

Wu Dingfang... Electrocuted to Death

Zhou Jaran... Should He Be Held Responsible?

Wu Dingfang, a local, was an apprentice at the Dasheng Printing House at No. 150 Zhoujiazui Road. At 2:00 PM on the 21st of this month, Wu walked barefoot through the printing shop and knocked over an electric fan. The fan was already damaged, which led to electrocution and death. After the Huishan Police Station investigated the cause of death, the manager of the printing house, Zhou Jaran from Taicang, was deemed to bear considerable responsibility as the owner of the shop. If the damaged electric fan had been repaired earlier, it would not have led to a fatal accident. Zhou was detained and sent to the Special District Court, which ordered him to be released on bail of 2,000 yuan pending trial. The trial opened yesterday morning. The police lawyer stated the facts, saying that Wu's death was caused by Zhou. As the saying goes, "Although I did not kill Boren, Boren died because of me." He should be punished. When Judge Feng asked Zhou, Zhou confessed. The verdict was not announced.

No Relatives Found, Photograph Taken for Identification

Rampant Bandits Outside Wusong Port

Counties Bordering the Sea Suffer Another Disaster

More Than Twenty People Kidnapped for Ransom

Outside Wusong Port, in the Da'an Port area bordering Tongzhou and Haimen, there are more than a thousand sea bandits gathered, with over a hundred bandit ships of various sizes. After Zhang Han, the fourth district chief of the Wusong water police, dispatched Captain Lin of the eighteenth squadron to lead patrol ships to jointly suppress the bandits with the Haimen County police, the bandits scattered to the outer sea. Unexpectedly, more than three hundred bandits sneaked ashore at Xinchang Town and looted everything. The day before yesterday, at around 5:00 AM, they sneaked to Lingdian Port and first went to the Public Security Bureau, seizing more than ten guns and injuring three policemen. Then, they surrounded the entire town and carried out large-scale looting, resulting in losses of about 40,000 yuan. They kidnapped more than twenty men and women for ransom, including Feng Jiming, Hong Jinkang, and Xu Dasheng. They then went to Yuehe Port and Xingang, looting them one after another, and fled to the area of Lusi Port. Another group of sea bandits, in more than ten sailing ships, invaded Xinxin Town in Qidongbei. Another group occupied Dajia Town in Haimen. Currently, the authorities in each county have dispatched police to block them. They are also convening military and police forces to discuss suppression measures.

Hope for Reconciliation in Rent Increase at Yile Lane

Yile Lane on Tangshan Road in Hongkou, this city, previously experienced opposition due to the landlord increasing rent, as reported in this newspaper. Subsequently, representatives of the lane's tenant association, Wang Huitang and Ye Yunping, mediated the matter. The landlord, the owner of Dingkang Qianzhuang (money shop), no longer held as intense a position as before. At the same time, they also stated that they would absolutely not take the rent increase as an issue, but due to the water company having raised prices and the increase in land taxes by the Public Works Department, they had no choice but to do so. Now, with your mediation, I will also consider the livelihoods of the residents."
