Two Fists Kill a Man

Over Three Yuan for Clothes

Chen Han, a woman from Chongming, is twenty-six years old. Her husband has passed away for many years. She inherited the carpentry business at No. 2, Lane 87, South Street, Hai Chao Temple, outside Xiaonanmen. The business is quite prosperous. She has a younger brother named Han Amao, who is twenty-three years old and very strong. He used to be a street paver. He has no family, so he lives with his sister. Last year, through an acquaintance's introduction, she employed an apprentice named Shi Caiyuan at the store. Unexpectedly, the apprentice suddenly ran away last month. She asked people to search for him everywhere, but he could not be found. Recently, she learned that the apprentice had been recommended by Ni Wenlang, a Chongming native, to Bian Erlang, a native of Haimen, who works as a sawyer at Chuanxinhe Bridge inside Ximen. Mrs. Chen and her brother Han Amao went to Bian to negotiate, wanting to bring Shi back. Bian agreed, but said that the apprentice had been here for a month, and the cost of food and lodging would not be discussed, but the three yuan he borrowed to make clothes should be returned. Mrs. Chen also agreed. Bian then asked Ni Wenlang to accompany them to get the money. When they arrived at Mrs. Chen's house, she suddenly changed her face and questioned Ni, "Why did you abduct my apprentice and sell him to someone else? Now you are trying to extort money." Ni also argued with her. Seeing that there were many carpenters, he was afraid of being at a disadvantage, so he endured it and retreated. He reported back to Bian. At around 10:00 AM yesterday, Bian and Ni went to Mrs. Chen's workshop to demand the three yuan for the clothes. Mrs. Chen refused to comply. At first, there was a verbal argument, and then a conflict broke out. Kong Xiande, a guard at the 26th post, heard about it and rushed to the scene. He saw Mrs. Chen's brother, Han Amao, violently punch Ni in the waist twice. Ni immediately fell to the ground in extreme pain, unconscious, and urinating and defecating. Police Kong arrested Han and took everyone involved back to the third precinct of the first district. At the same time, he quickly sent the injured man to Nanyang Hospital for treatment. The hospital found that Ni's injuries were severe and could not be treated, so they refused to admit him. He was then returned to Mrs. Chen's carpentry shop by car. He died on the way. Jin, the police chief, ordered Han and others to be interrogated. As the case involved human life, he ordered them to be sent to the Shanghai District Court for questioning. He then ordered the local chief to report to the court for an examination. At around 4:00 PM, Prosecutor Zhao, accompanied by forensic officials, arrived at the scene and examined the body. The deceased, Ni Wenlang, was covered in purple bruises. He died of fatal injuries sustained during the attack. He ordered the relatives of the deceased to sign a statement and collect the body for coffining. It is reported that the deceased, Ni Wenlang, was only twenty-seven years old and worked as a sawyer.

Three Child Laborers Claim to Have Gone to Cultivate Immortality

Mother of Tang Tong Almost Goes Insane

Tang Liusheng (16 years old) who lives in Beishenjiazhai, Longhua Town, West Shanghai, Xiao Henan (17 years old) who lives in Caohe Temple, and Lu Huxiang (21 years old) who lives in Shanxiali, Xiaomu Bridge, are all child laborers in the loading room of the Longhua Arsenal. It has been four years. Recently, the three children do not know what kind of magic they have been affected by, and they are obsessed with immortals. They often want to cultivate. They are usually devout in eating plain vegetarian food to repay their parents' kindness, and they must recite sutras and incantations every morning and evening. However, they are still working hard, so their families did not take it seriously. Unexpectedly, the night before yesterday, Tang, Xiao, and Lu did not return home. Yesterday morning, the Longhua Arsenal Labor Union suddenly received a registered letter in the name of Tang and other three children, with the factory symbol attached, requesting it to be returned on their behalf, and stating that they had all gone to cultivate immortality, and earnestly requesting someone to tell their families not to be sad. Upon inspecting the envelope, it was sent from the Minhang Post Office. After the labor union informed Tang Liusheng's old mother, Zhang, and the heads of the Xiao and Lu families, they learned the truth, cried loudly, and immediately took the Shanghai-Minhang bus to find them, but there was no trace. According to the locals, yesterday afternoon, three people wearing Su blue cloth short shirts and trousers, resembling child laborers, were seen passing through the streets, but it is unknown where they went. Therefore, the three families of Tang and others returned crying in pain. However, Tang Liusheng's mother, Zhang, suffered a great shock to her nerves after losing her son. She did not eat or drink every day, and searched everywhere, in an extremely pitiful state. It is hoped that kind people everywhere, if they see the three children, will please notify the Xinchun Garden in front of Longhua Great Temple. If the flesh and blood are reunited, it will be a great good thing.

Art World

Literature of Poland

Before the European War, Poland, like India and Egypt, suffered the fate of national subjugation. Despite several revolutions under the yoke of Russia, Germany, and Austria, it could not escape the fate of being a forcefully controlled and suppressed nation. However, after the war in Europe, it gained independence. In its journey to fight for freedom and independence, we cannot ignore the revolutionary poets and writers who fueled the Polish revolution. They stirred up the oppressed Polish nation in their songs, fought and struggled in the wars that overthrew the rule of Russia, Germany, and Austria, and shone with extraordinary brilliance in the dark era of the nineteenth century.

The mid-nineteenth century was the golden age of Polish literature. The first poet who could be called the Polish Dante was Adam Mickiewicz. His creations, like the tragedy of his country, were subjected to unexpected changes. He was imprisoned and exiled in Russia and foreign lands. Therefore, his works also changed due to the stimulation of the environment. In prison, he abandoned rosy dreams and gave up the praise of fleeting love, transforming his early melancholic tone into a lament for the collective misfortune of his nation. Later, in the war against Russian rule, he sang of the bravery of soldiers and the glory of death, although his own destiny was accompanied by the same misfortune as the defeated. But his greatness was admired by all Polish people. Moreover, he wrote the national epic "Mr. Thaddeus" about the failure of the Polish people's hope that Napoleon would defeat Russia. It implicitly contains the cloud that unfortunately enveloped his country, everyone's hope for victory in war, and the hope for the revival of the Polish nation that filled the hearts of the Polish people, all vividly presented. Therefore, in order to realize his doctrine of the resurrection of the motherland, he did not hesitate to organize the Polish army to help other countries attack their main enemies, Russia and Austria. Although he died before facing the enemy, he was always a leader of thought for all Polish people, forever occupying the position of a prophet, and guiding beyond literature. He was the first writer in Poland to gain practical experience in reality.

In contrast to Mickiewicz's career was the poet Juliusz Słowacki. In the success of art and literature, although he used poetry as a tool to imply national thought and religious philosophy, he paid attention to human emotions in the vast material. Therefore, in the unfinished long epic "Beniowski," he discussed international and national religious, philosophical, literary, and social issues. In the poems "At Sunset on the Sea" and "Agamemnon's Grave," he deeply expressed sorrow for the fate of the country divided by violence and coercion, and the wandering of the people, giving people a strong emotional stimulus in sorrow. Therefore, in terms of realism, he was better able to write about the encounters of the entire Polish nation. Therefore, examining his entire works, "The King Spirit" narrates the spirit of the motherland presented during the rule of various countries, "Kordian" writes about the panorama of Poland during the 1830 revolution, and "Anhelli" is a complete depiction of the Polish nation under the partition of the Russian, German, and Austrian empires, describing the suffering of Polish prisoners exiled in the cold Siberian prison. He was as famous as Mickiewicz in the same era. In the Polish literature of the nineteenth and even the twentieth centuries, the few poets who could best express revolutionary enthusiasm apart from romanticism and realism were either decadent or pessimistic. Therefore, of the three great romanticists, in addition to the two of them, there was also Zygmunt Krasiński. Although he was a serious poet who did not deeply think about philosophical human events, in "Psalm of Faith" he recalled Poland's painful past and its future mission, and "Psalm of Hope," which predicted future success, described the human love necessary in revolution and terror, and "Psalm of Love" are all immortal works. However, the harvest in realism was not as great as that given by the romantic poets. The female poet Mary Konopnicka was a singer of the pain of workers, peasants, and the oppressed, with democracy as her backbone. Bolesław Prus was a humanitarian novelist with democratic ideas who sympathized with the common people. However, Henryk Sienkiewicz was the one who gained world reputation from Poland's standpoint.

Henryk Sienkiewicz was the greatest writer in Poland in recent times. The latter half of the nineteenth century was entirely his world for twenty-five years. He was famous for writing historical novels. Apart from some works with a pessimistic tone, his works expressing Poland were also very great. The novel "The Lighthouse Keeper" describes a Polish exile who was a lighthouse keeper in the West Indies. He was dismissed for neglecting his duties because he read Mickiewicz's poems and fell into longing for his homeland, reflecting the sorrow of the subjugated. "Mr. Wołodyjowski" writes about the bravery of resisting the Turks on the front line. "Fire and Sword" writes about the story of the Polish people defending against the Cossack invasion. "The Diary of a Schoolmaster" writes about the oppression given to them by the Russian Empire. "Bartek the Conqueror" contains a strong Polish national spirit.

The above group of writers were all figures active in the environment of experiential philosophical thought. They once set up landmarks and pillars in popular culture, established a new era in literature, indicated that the Polish nation had surpassed the spirit of class, accommodated the common people into the splendid "Pantheon," and used the aristocratic epic skills to describe all the suffering and misfortune of the harmed. After the failure of experiential philosophy, the entire literary world gradually became occupied by the high-minded and impressionists who sang "art for art's sake," and there were no great productions until recent years. All that existed were merely works of art.

After the death of the old writer Henryk Sienkiewicz, in the past ten years, Władysław Reymont shouted out the voice of resistance from the oppressed, Stefan Żeromski put forward the literature of individual resistance as a social appendage, and Stanisław Przybyszewski and the humanitarian Jan Kasprowicz died one after another. This group of poets, influenced by the humanitarianism of the deceased Jan Kasprowicz, gathered in Warsaw to publish the "Skamander" journal to promote everything of international poets. However, in Warsaw, there was also a group of young poets who used national legends as their themes to promote the national spirit. They had a deep feeling for their hometown, and everything was based on local myths, ballads, and customs. Under the leadership of their journal "Czartak," they advocated using simple, primitive language and artistic methods to express the national spirit. They took the poet Emil Zegadłowicz as their representative, forming a reflection with the new Polish international poet Julian Tuwim. In these two major trends, due to Poland's international status, the nationalist young poets were more welcomed by the people. (Yi Kang)

Literary Anecdotes

Hawthorne, Tired of Socializing

Hawthorne was the most solitary of modern American writers. However, while he hated socializing with others, he was particularly close to Emerson.

Emerson fully understood Hawthorne's temperament. Apart from socializing with Emerson, Hawthorne hated interacting with all other writers. He thought it was more interesting to play funny games with captains, workers, and sailors than to interact with writers.

Although he and Emerson met frequently, they didn't say much apart from what was necessary. And Emerson was also very silent. Therefore, even when they met, the words they spoke could be counted.

When Markley and Hitnis Smith met, the two people just sat opposite each other without saying a word. The two mouths were sealed as if one hour, two hours, or even three hours passed. Perhaps everyone knows this story.

But Hawthorne and Emerson were even more formidable than this pair after all. (Ping)

(1) Texts are limited to news, reviews, and introductions of recent art (including painting, music, sculpture, architecture, drama, etc.) and literature at home and abroad.

(3) Photos are limited to recent portraits and works of domestic and foreign writers and various photographs related to writing.

Book and Newspaper Introductions

Lakeside Song, A Great Narrative Poem

By Mu Hong, published by Nanhua Bookstore

Night comes, catching the ashen night,

I am marching in an already stirring dream. Under my feet are two paths—

One called the red war, one called the red love.

Some list me among Satan's group,

Others call me the star of salvation,

But all I have is more than just these monotonous titles,

Because my heart is something I myself don't understand.

It's just that the old era gave me depression and pain, and future dreams gave me longing and pursuit.

I am a struggling child in life. I can't help my heart beating…

Although the torch of yesterday has gone out, the east is not yet bright,

Although the great dream of this morning has just broken, the rooster's crow has not yet been heard.

What to say about war, and what about love?

I am here, having lived through ordinary storms…

I have gone crazy once or twice in war,

I have also gone crazy once or twice in love.

It is precisely the wings of love and war

That have grown horizontally from under my ribs.

What cannot be forgotten is the infatuation of the beauty,

What cannot be avoided is the majestic shadow of the lake and mountains.

The beauty, the lake and mountains, the lake and mountains, the beauty,

………………………………

The above is the first section of the prelude to Lakeside Song

Mentioning this great narrative poem, I can't help but think of the time I spent with the poet Mu Hong. That was in the winter of the seventeenth year, when we lived in the pavilion room of a certain alley on North Sichuan Road for two or three months. Mu Hong, like all true poets, was silent, gentle, beautiful, and also had keen observation, good reason, and the most ardent passion. His burly, northern-type body almost touched the low ceiling when he stood up. He often sat silently in front of the bed. The room was too small. We couldn't put another orange between the bed and the table, so he had to lean over the table or lie down. Smiles never left his face, just like the morning sun that never left the horizon, making a smile in the golden clouds. His good reason was often observing his inner life, and he related to people with a child-like purity. Just spending a period of life with him, I felt that my temperament had changed a lot. He didn't often read books, and rarely picked up a pen to write anything. Often for several months, except for writing letters—which was also rare—he didn't write. But the books he read in a week exceeded what we read in a month. Every one of his works was completed in the shortest period of time. "Red Sun" took nine days, "Lakeside Song" took three days. Thinking about completing such a great work in three days is almost a miracle.

Once, a friend told us the following story, which was said to be a true story that happened in Dongting Lake a few years ago. He borrowed that story to write this work, asking me to write a novel with the same story, saying that our works could be published together in the future. But after reading his poem, I could no longer write a single word, until now. Last year, I released this poem at the Nanhua Bookstore, and even the promised preface was not written, because this poem was too huge a giant in front of me, and I couldn't add anything to it.

This is a truly Chinese thing, a Chinese story, singing about the passionate love of Chinese people, using the Chinese style. He completed Chinese poetry, raised the banner of romance, and declared to the world with this poem, "Look, there are some truly great things here that are ours. From here, you can understand the soul of China. Here, our past is contained, and our future is also displayed." It sings about war and love, the peak of human activity, just like everything that romance sings about. However, what is different from the old romance and the new Marxist romance is that there is not such a strong color of heroism and individualism. Our hero, carrying war and love on both sides, is indeed a hero, but he is also such an ordinary person. He is just like our brother, like the people we often approach. He lives in a legendary situation, but his life is so close to us. This is a declaration belonging to mankind, a march towards the perfect future of mankind, igniting the flames of hot blood in the banner of our nation, pure light and full enthusiasm.

This long poem of more than three thousand lines is written in a beautiful tone, like a melodious song, and like the most fluent prose. It has an attractive force that makes you have to talk to the last line after opening the book, and after reading it, it will always occupy your mind. The most beautiful, and at the same time the most powerful. If a foreigner asks me about Chinese poets and poems, I will not hesitate to mention "Lakeside Song" and its author first (secondly, I will mention Ke Zhongping's "Sea Night Song" and "Molin—Malin").

This is a great poem, like all great poems—there is no doctrine, no dogma, no politics, and no socialism, whether correct or false. It is impossible to find anything in it that can be written as a declaration or slogan, so it is impossible to criticize it with these. It is written with the soul of mankind—but according to behaviorism, not only is there no soul, but there is no heart. Then I should say it is written with the entire spirit of mankind, with the bright behavior of mankind, all the same. In here, how strongly the spirit of our nation, the largest part of mankind (excluding the number of yellow people gathered under China, that is to say, they all have some important common characteristics, and the number of people who can be represented by the term China is the largest), is displayed here.

The story of the narrative poem is roughly as follows. A vagrant sings of his life experience. Because of the pressure of opportunity, he went to the lake and occupied the area, becoming the leader of the bandits. With his bright heart and ardent emotions, he swept through the heart of the lake and the shore like a breeze blowing in Jingjiang. Accidentally, because of the sound of the pipa, he unconsciously aroused the heart of a married woman. Immediately, strong love occurred between them. He risked danger and did everything to be his lover. Therefore, on the one hand, it was entangled love, and on the other hand, it was constant war. But the hero on the lake finally could not resist the long-term pressure of the official government. Because of an internal agent, the career disintegrated. She disguised herself and went to prison to see her—and then said goodbye forever, embarking on his wandering journey.

The poem is too beautiful, I can't quote it, I'm afraid I've written too much. Now I'll just record the last paragraph to end my humble article.

I am now in—

In this bleak night,

Still forgetting the pain,

Because—

That love, in front of me,

—Longing…

You, you,

Your face,

Lotus,

Your smile,

Red as the sun,

Your eyebrows,

Green as the mountains,

Your entire waist,

Rainbow on the sea,

No beautiful description…

Your hands,

White jade carved like a painting,

Warm and like a heart,

Also like the sound in the lake…

The trembling shadow in the heart of the water…

Night light, frog sound, water sound, grass movement…

All your symbols

You are the spirit of beauty,

—Night,

—Night,

—Deeply,

—Heavily,

Secretly—

Intentionally, unintentionally,

We met,

Met,

With love,

Reborn,

Born again from tomorrow,

The spirit of mankind,

Born again from tomorrow,

Our new heart—

New love,

There's more below, but I won't quote it anymore, because such beautiful chapters can't be copied completely, and the night is very late.

Our poet is now in his hometown, in the embrace of nature, in poverty. I haven't written to him for a long time. This little bit of my humble work is not worth offering to him. It's just enough to express my admiration and remembrance. August of the nineteenth year, Pei Liang.

European Writers' New Works in Review: Angioletta (11)

— Man Ru

A Play by the Spanish Azorín

In the past, people in China who wrote novels and plays had an old saying called, "If the book is not enough, the Bodhisattva will come to make it up." The meaning is that when the plot reaches a point where the author can't get out of it, only asking the Bodhisattva and gods to come and turn things around can it be done. Therefore, in old novels and old dramas, we often see the protagonist encountering difficulties, and suddenly a savior comes from the sky. This method, of course, exposes the weakness of the technique, but it is very convenient for the author. Therefore, that old saying not only expresses the superficiality of old novels and old dramas, but it is still applicable today. In the West, this situation has not disappeared, but that was still in the Middle Ages. It was completely eradicated in the eighteenth century. Moreover, the "Miracle Play" of the Middle Ages mostly used the Bodhisattva as an important character, which is also a bit different from the use of the Bodhisattva as a floating bridge in our old literature.

The disappearance of gods and miracles from the Western stage and the pens of playwrights has been two or three hundred years. But recently, miracles seem to have started yawning on the European stage, preparing to be resurrected. Because the Spanish playwright Azorín not only gave the first yawn to miracles in his recent play, but also clearly declared that miracles must be resurrected on the European stage.

The fact is this: Azorín, a prolific and exquisite Spanish writer, recently wrote a play, "Angelita." In this play, he applied "miracles," and applied them very well. As for this short play, it is both energetic and charming, and can undoubtedly be regarded as one of his masterpieces. However, it is difficult to say whether the success of this play is due to the use of miracles or has nothing to do with miracles, because these two are mixed together and cannot be separated. However, the author's claim is that miracles and wonders, which were expelled from the stage in the eighteenth century, should return to the stage, because "after the tangible and obvious reality, there exists another more subtle, more real, more permanent reality."

The protagonist, Angioletta, is concerned about her own future destiny and eager to predict it. She gets a jade ring. Wearing this ring, rotating it once can move her forward one year. She is very impatient and spins the ring twice, so her age increases by two years. She finds herself married, but because things happen too quickly, she gets confused and mistakenly recognizes her father-in-law as her husband, and her husband as an outsider. Later, she rotates the ring five times, and suddenly finds that her house has been transformed into a hospital for heart patients. Finally, she meets three Angiolettas, two of whom (one is a female New York journalist, and one is the wife of a certain scientist) disappear, and the third transforms into the existing Angioletta. But Angioletta at this time is a woman who has lost a lot but has become much smarter.

In this era where the scientific world is changing a lot and scientists have many new studies on time and space, we don't need to criticize a writer for playing this trick with time. Moreover, Azorín's work has a light and gentle style, the characters are clearly personalized, and the dialogue is fast and natural throughout the play.

Guidelines for Book and Newspaper Introduction Submissions

(1) Texts are limited to introductions of the latest publications at home and abroad. In addition to literary works, all political, economic, legal, scientific, educational, etc. books and newspapers are included in the introduction, but boring books and newspapers will not be introduced.

(2) Pictures are limited to recent works by new domestic and foreign writers and accompanying illustrations related to the text.

(3) Articles on textual research or research on ancient Chinese books will not be published.

(4) Pictures and photos are limited to those related to the text.

(5) Each text should not exceed three thousand words at most.

(6) Do not write on both sides of the manuscript paper.

(7) Do not write manuscripts horizontally, and do not write characters in a sloppy manner. Western texts can be omitted where possible. If it is necessary to quote the original text, it must be attached below the translation.

Business News

The New World Hotel in Nichengqiao announced that the hotel's business has been unusually prosperous since the summer, which is unprecedented among hotels. This is because the location is central, the transportation is convenient, the location is adjacent to the racecourse, the air is sufficient, the furnishings are elegant and clean, and the pricing is low. In addition, the newly added rooftop garden and cold food, white vegetable dishes, etc. are convenient for travelers. After autumn, the heat has not diminished, and there are more and more people who tend to it, which is regarded as an idyllic paradise. Therefore, the hotel's business is becoming more and more prosperous.

The Huaxin Company in the central city of Nanjing Road announced that since the company held the autumn discount, the business has suddenly become prosperous. The goods are new and unique, and the selling price is also fair and unusual. The most popular and purchased by customers is the beautiful new clothes in the new clothing department, new silk clothing materials, the artistic spring leather shoes in the shoe department, and the large number of silk stockings from famous Chinese factories in the sock department. The rest are cosmetics, suits, leather bags, clips, towels, and jewelry, which are also very lively. Now, in order to reward customers, it does not hesitate to make major sacrifices, and specially reduces the price of pure silk stockings from famous Chinese factories to 85 cents per pair, various clips to 40 cents per dozen, top-quality undershirts to three pieces per dollar, embroidered women's shoes to one dollar per pair, and Indian silk cheongsam materials to four dollars per piece. The rest of the goods are generally discounted from 30% to 10%.

News from the Publishing World

The book The Life and Thought of Ancient and Modern Philosophers was originally written by Dr. Will Durant in the United States, and is now translated into Chinese by Yang Yinhong and Yinweikun. It is a hard-covered volume of more than 800 pages and more than 300,000 words. The material is very rich and the writing is fluent. It is indeed a famous book. This book is widely sold in Europe and the United States. Scholars of philosophy must read it. It is sold in various branches of the Commercial Press and major bookstores.

He also specializes in seal script and landscape painting, inheriting Wen and Shen, and connecting the Four Wangs. He is elegant and natural. Pine and plum are also quite antique. He lives at No. 49 Chenxiangge Road in Xinbeimen. The major stationery and fan shops are collection points.
